3009   𝐿( 21 + 𝑖𝑦, Sym𝑟 𝜋 × 𝜏) = 0 — the carrier’s exact zero-detector, fiber-parametric, reading only the signed-
3010   channel/lane geometry. This detects the vanishing set; it does not by itself establish pole-absence —
3011   entireness is the separate completeness statement of Lemma 60.

3012   Proof. 𝑅 𝑟,𝜏 is read through the configured carrier+fiber system, in the causal order configuration
3013   → realization → closure → rank-drop → factorization. The rank-drop is a loss of a state-space
3014   degree of freedom, not the vanishing of a separate coefficient. Frobenius balance. The harmonized
3015   payload carries the passport stamps (F) Frobenius balance and (S) vanishing-sign compatibility
3016   — the determinant character (det 𝜑𝜏,𝑣 )𝑟+1 of Lemma 62 being booked into the warp, not left
3017   to drift — so by Lemma 58 its strand residuals are opposite, 𝑅 + = −𝑅 − , and no unpaired
3018   determinant residue enters the cell. Configuration. The fiber’s coefficients split the reflected
3019   readout into the signed positive and negative phasor channels 𝑃𝑟,𝜏 (𝑦), 𝑀𝑟,𝜏 (𝑦) (the 𝐴, 𝐵 channels,

       pencil 𝐿 = 𝜇𝐴 𝜆𝐵 (HarmonicPencilCell.focalKernel_cell_eq_AB_det). Realization and height.

3023   (represented point 12 + 𝑖 𝑦, HarmonicPencilCell.reprPoint). Closure correspondence. A vanishing
3024   of the readout is full signed-channel cancellation, hence focal coincidence of the two lane states:
3025   Φ𝑟,𝜏 (𝑦) = 0 ⇐⇒ 𝑃𝑟,𝜏 (𝑦) = 𝑀𝑟,𝜏 (𝑦) ⇐⇒ 𝑋+ (𝑒 𝑦 ) = 𝑋− (𝑒 𝑦 ) (focal_zero_iff_scalar_zero).
3026   Rank-drop. At coincidence the two lane vectors are linearly dependent, so det 𝐿c = (𝜆 − 𝜇)𝐴𝐵 = 0,
3027   and the Hermitian PSD Gram matrix drops rank, det 𝐺c = | det 𝐿c | 2 = 0 (gramH_posSemidef,

3034   detection — the pencil marks the vanishing set; pole-absence (entireness) is the separate DC/constant
3035   mode, established from completeness in Lemma 60. The detector is fiber-parametric and does
3036   not require any zero of Φ𝑟,𝜏 to exist: it reads no global Weil–Galois parameter (so it holds for
3037   Maass 𝜏) and no automorphy of Sym𝑟 𝜋. Machine-checked for the Dirichlet model; the same
3038   determinant-one lane balance for the general symmetric-power/twist fiber, realized as forcible
3039   closure with a machine-checked controllability core (Lemma 61). Away from a coincidence the
3040   smallest singular value reopens, 𝜎min (𝐺 c (𝑡)) ∼ 𝐶 |𝑡 − 𝑡0 | 𝑘 — the post-closure resistance below, a
3041   recovery rate, not a residual mode.                                                                     □
3042   Lemma 60 (Entireness from completeness: the residue is the trivial-channel coefficient). For the
3043   configured tensor fiber 𝑊𝑟,𝜏 with coefficients 𝜆𝑛 , the constant term of the 𝑥 → 0+ expansion of the carrier
       theta 𝐾 𝑟,𝜏 (𝑥) = 𝑛 𝜆𝑛 𝑔(𝑛𝑥) — the Riemann–Hecke residual 𝑅 𝑟,𝜏 , equal by the Mellin pair to the edge
                        Í
3044

3045   residue of Λ(𝑠) — is the DC/zero-frequency mode of the bank, i.e. its coefficient mean. Every nontrivial
3046   channel of the self-compatible cell has zero cell-mean (CommonRepresentation.harmonize_char), so
3047   𝑅 𝑟,𝜏 equals the trivial-channel coefficient alone (complete_bank_dc_zero). Hence if 𝑊𝑟,𝜏 carries
3048   no trivial channel — completeness — then 𝑅 𝑟,𝜏 = 0 and Λ(𝑠, Sym𝑟 𝜋 × 𝜏) is entire. For non-
3049   exceptional 𝜋 the tensor Sym𝑟 𝜑𝜋 ⊗ 𝜑𝜏 has no trivial constituent whenever dim 𝜑𝜏 < dim Sym𝑟 𝜑𝜋
3050   (TrivialChannel.no_nonzero_hom_of_finrank_lt, a dimension count — no automorphy of Sym𝑟 𝜋


                                                           86
3051   used), so 𝑊𝑟,𝜏 is complete and the twist is entire. The exceptional/reducible 𝜋 carry a genuine trivial
3052   constituent — the classical 𝜁-factor pole — and Sym𝑟 𝜋 is then the known isobaric object (§16).

3053   Proof. By absolute convergence (𝜆𝑛 = 𝑂(𝑛 𝐴 )) the Mellin pair is exact on Re 𝑠 > 𝜎0 , so the 𝑥 → 0+
3054   constant term of 𝐾 𝑟,𝜏 is the residue of ℳ𝐾 𝑟,𝜏 (𝑠) = Λ(𝑠) at the edge (Riemann–Hecke) — the DC
3055   Fourier coefficient of the bank. Decomposing the coefficients into the fiber’s channels (additive
3056   characters of the self-compatible cell group), character orthogonality gives that each nontrivial
3057   channel sums to zero over a cell (harmonize_char), so the DC coefficient is the trivial-channel
3058   coefficient alone (complete_bank_dc_zero). A trivial channel is present iff 𝜑𝜏∨ embeds in Sym𝑟 𝜑𝜋
3059   (a trivial constituent); for non-exceptional 𝜋 with dim 𝜑𝜏 < dim Sym𝑟 𝜑𝜋 that Hom-space is zero
3060   (no_nonzero_hom_of_finrank_lt), so there is no trivial channel, 𝑅 𝑟,𝜏 = 0, and Λ is entire. The
                          c =𝑉 Φ
       pencil residual 𝐷𝑟,𝜏
3061                             𝑟,𝜏 𝑟,𝜏 of Lemma 59 is a separate quantity — the zero-detector, the readout’s
3062   value along the line — not this DC/residue mode; the two must not be conflated.                      □
3063   Cell closure is not a fiber-uniform theorem to be proved once for all functions, but a property of each
3064   carrier+fiber pair, effected by the fiber’s own adapted warp — the same split as “the carrier sets the
3065   functional equation, the fiber sets the function”. For the class of finite duality-stable harmonic fibers —
3066   those whose weight channels are 𝑃-th roots of unity, none trivial — this closure is proved in Lean, at the
3067   weight level and Galois-free: each nonzero-weight channel cancels over its native cell by the geomet-
       ric series 𝑘<𝑃 𝜁 𝑘 = 0 (CellClosure.root_of_unity_cell_sum_zero), so the warped bank closes
                   Í
3068

3069   (harmonic_bank_cell_sum_zero) and its primitive is bounded (harmonic_bank_primitive_bounded),
3070   whence 𝐴car = 𝑂(1), the vertical bound, and 𝑅 𝑟,𝜏 = 0 (cell_closure_dc_mode_zero). The Dirichlet
3071   characters of any conductor — the 𝜒3 archetype of §34 included — are the classical instances
3072   (dirichlet_cell_closure, recovering character_partialSum_norm_le). A cuspidal fiber, whose
3073   Satake angles are not roots of unity, is not in this harmonic class: at the base scale its cells do not
3074   close. At its own harmonic scale the controllability theorem ForcibleClosure.residual_forcible
3075   can close an individual residual once two independent correction directions are supplied. This
3076   does not show that the ordinary coefficient primitive is bounded or that an 𝑛-dependent in-
3077   verse warp has summable variation. Placing both ordinary completed readouts on an open
3078   strip therefore requires the raw primitive hypothesis of Lemma 66 or the kernel hypotheses of
3079   InverseWarpKernelTransfer.inverseWarp_transfer_tendsto; machine-checked end-to-end for
3080   the character classes (dirichlet_strip_tendsto_LFunction), classical for holomorphic GL(2), and
3081   independently evidenced by the discriminating instruments (the oracle-free critical-line readout to
3082   2 × 10−16 , the growth locator to 10−12 , the FE closures, App. B). Warp controllability itself (Lemma 61)
3083   contributes only the arithmetic-neutral transport half — it closes cells at any admissible fiber’s own
3084   scale, consuming none of the fiber’s arithmetic, which is exactly what universal transport requires
3085   of it (Cor. 76) and exactly why it is not niceness evidence: force-closure alone yields no continuation
3086   to transfer. The axis-reality reflection (Lemma 71) consumes this continuation; the residual mode
3087   vanishes by completeness (Lemma 60), unconditionally; and full-plane entireness then follows
3088   from the entire reflected carrier theta, downstream of the functional equation — the dependency
3089   order of Lemma 71, no step feeding on its successor. What is exhibited per instance is then only
3090   the finer warp dynamics — the post-closure resistance below — never the entireness. There is no
3091   fiber-independent cancellation for the carrier to prove, because the carrier never faces a function
3092   without its fiber.

3093   Lemma 61 (Forcible cell closure via the reachable independent stage). For a cuspidal fiber the adapted
3094   warp that closes a cell need not be found by luck, and the two independent correction directions need not occur
3095   at every native cell. The readout-preserving warp carries a few coherent generators — the winding Ω(𝑛),
       the distinct-prime count 𝜔(𝑛), the vertical shift log 𝑛, and the fiber’s own local periods Θ(𝑛) = 𝑝 𝑘 ∥𝑛 𝑘 𝜃𝑝
                                                                                                           Í
3096




                                                             87
3097   (arithmetic functions and the fiber’s finite local data, not arbitrary per-term phases) — whose real weights
       drive the cell residual 𝐷𝐶 = 𝑛∈𝐶 𝑎 𝑛 𝜔𝑊 (𝑛). The controllability core is exact and machine-checked: two R-
                                       Í
3098

3099   linearly-independent warp correction-directions 𝑢, 𝑣 span the residual plane C, so every residual 𝐷 is forcible
3100   to zero by real weights, 𝐷 + (𝑠 ·𝑢 + 𝑡 ·𝑣) = 0 (ForcibleClosure.residual_forcible, Lean. Those two
3101   directions are not demanded cell by cell. By CarrierReachability.reachable_independent_stage,
3102   every nontrivial admissible fiber (continuous non-constant lane phase 𝜙) admits a reachable carrier stage — a
3103   height 𝑦 with sin(2𝜙(𝑦)) ≠ 0 — at which the two dual lanes 𝑒 ±𝑖𝜙(𝑦) are R-linearly independent. No transport
3104   of the cell is involved: the residual 𝐷𝐶 is a fixed scalar, and the stage supplies the correction pair 𝑢 = 𝑒 𝑖𝜙(𝑦) ,
3105   𝑣 = 𝑒 −𝑖𝜙(𝑦) ; residual_forcible applied to that pair gives real weights 𝑠, 𝑡 with 𝐷𝐶 + 𝑠 𝑢 + 𝑡 𝑣 = 0, exactly.
3106   Thus per-cell closure follows from global carrier reachability supplying one independent pair, not from
3107   cell-by-cell linear independence. The two machine-checked inputs are reachable_independent_stage
3108   and residual_forcible their composition is the direct application of the second to the pair the first supplies,
3109   in prose here, not a further Lean theorem. The constructive rate is what the numerics exhibit, in the carrier’s
3110   own chart: on native growth cells — uniform in 𝑦 = log 𝑍, every phasor entering at zero magnitude through
3111   the canonical 𝐶 ∞ growth window, no clipped edge — exact Gauss–Newton closes |𝐷𝐶 | to the float64 floor
3112   (median 5 × 10−15 –1.4 × 10−14 ) on every cell of all three fibers, 30/30 each, with weights |𝑥| ≤ 3.1, once the
3113   generator suite includes the fiber’s own local periods Θ(𝑛); the three arithmetic generators alone already close
3114   30/30 on Δ and Sym5 Δ, leaving one rank-deficient Sym13 cell that Θ closes — the resisting cell naming its
3115   adapter. (The clip control that makes the never-clip method law measurable is documented in App. B.)

3116   This realizes the cell closure of Lemma 59 constructively for the cuspidal fiber: each cell is forced
3117   closed, so no zero-frequency mode survives — an explicit constructive mechanism whose algebraic
3118   core (two independent directions force any residual) is machine-checked and supplied by the reach-
3119   able independent stage, not cell by cell, behind the structural rank-drop. Scope, fixed by the theorem’s
3120   own generality: controllability is arithmetic-neutral — residual_forcible consumes no arithmetic,
3121   closing cells for every admissible fiber — so it is the transport half of the architecture, consumed by
3122   universality (Cor. 76, Thm. 75 (c)) and by the adapter suite, not niceness evidence; within niceness its
3123   role is to book the per-cell correction, while the arithmetic enters through the inverse-warp transfer
3124   of §37. Its controllability and reachability legs are proved (ForcibleClosure.residual_forcible,
3125   CarrierReachability.reachable_independent_stage); the inverse-kernel summability and bound-
3126   ary legs are separately exposed by InverseWarpKernelTransfer.inverseWarp_transfer_tendsto.
3127   A universal bounded-weight per-cell claim would be false on the rank-deficient locus and, be-
3128   ing arithmetic-neutral, needs no strengthening for the chain. The boundary is sharp, and not
3129   where a first reading places it. The residual factorization is unconditional: 𝐷𝐶 = 𝑉 Φ with 𝑉 ≠ 0
3130   — the Gram-pencil rank-drop leaving no zero-frequency mode independent of the readout —
3131   is a channel-agnostic identity in (𝐴, 𝐵, 𝜇, 𝜆), machine-checked in Lean for arbitrary channels
3132   (HarmonicCell.harmonic_residual_no_independent_mode and instantiated end-to-end for the
3133   Dirichlet model; it reads only the fiber’s own P/M channels, so it holds verbatim for every det-one
3134   symmetric-power/twist fiber, Maass included. The finer constructive reachability — that the dual
3135   carrier admits a reachable stage whose two lane directions are R-linearly independent, demanded
3136   once rather than at every cell — governs the closure dynamics, not the vanishing of the residual
3137   mode, and it too is settled rather than left to numerics. The required two correction directions are
3138   not obtained by a genericity argument. For the dual carrier they are the two lanes 𝑒 ±𝑖𝜙(𝑦) of the helix,
3139   and a complex number and its conjugate are R-linearly independent at a carrier height 𝑦 exactly
3140   when sin(2𝜙(𝑦)) ≠ 0 (independent iff off the axes, not merely 𝜙 ≠ 0 — at 𝜙 = 𝜋/2 the two lanes
3141   coincide up to sign). The complete dual helix runs continuously 0 → ∞ on both lanes, so a clock
3142   with sin(2𝜙) ≡ 0 would map the connected line into the discrete set 𝜋2 Z and hence be constant —
3143   the DC/trivial lock. A nontrivial (non-constant) admissible clock therefore attains some height with


                                                               88
3144   sin(2𝜙) ≠ 0: CarrierReachability.reachable_independent_stage proves that every nontrivial
3145   source fiber in the stated structural class (continuous non-constant 𝜙) admits a carrier stage with two
3146   R-linearly-independent lane directions, and ForcibleClosure.residual_forcible then yields
3147   the exact correction. Both are machine-checked: completeness supplies the continuous 0 → ∞
3148   carrier, admissibility the structured non-random clock, and nontriviality excludes the constant
3149   lock. So reachability is unconditional on the nontrivial admissible source class, not a numerical
3150   input; the numerics (Sym5 –Sym13 , the twisted family) are calibration. Boundedness likewise does not
3151   ride on the forcing. The vertical-strip bound is structural, from the Euler factor: on its convergence
3152   domain the full helix is the convergent product of local factors det(1 − 𝐴 𝑝 𝑞 −𝑠  𝑝 ) , each a bounded
                                                                                             −1

3153   rational function with |𝐴 𝑝 | polynomially bounded (Kim–Sarnak for 𝜋, Jacquet–Shalika/LRS for
3154   𝜏), so the readout is finite order there; the functional equation extends that bound across the strip
3155   (Lemma 64), given entireness — independent of the forcing chart. Hence the per-cell forcing weights
3156   need not be bounded for 𝐿 to be finite order (in the native growth chart the measured closing
3157   weights are in fact 𝑂(1)–𝑂(3); only the clipped control chart inflates them — either way a feature of
3158   the constructive route, not a bound on 𝐿). Forcible closure thus makes the cell closure constructive;
3159   entireness rests on completeness (Lemma 60), boundedness on the Euler factor, and reachability
3160   on the completeness–admissibility argument above — so no leg of niceness rests on numerics; the
3161   tested families confirm the mechanism rather than carry it.
3162        Functorial preservation — and its limit. That reachability is not isolated per fiber. Exact focal
3163   closure is preserved under the carrier’s structural transports — composition, Rankin–Selberg ten-
3164   sor, and base change: if two transports each carry closure to closure, so does their composite
3165   (CarrierFunctoriality.faithful_comp, Lean, no axioms; with the associativity, two-sided iden-
3166   tity, and base-change law bc𝑝 ◦ bc𝑞 = bc𝑝𝑞 of §40), and the plethysm splits each composite exactly
3167   into irreducible Sym𝑐 blocks (Sym2 ◦ Sym2 = Sym4 ⊕ Sym0 , Sym3 ◦ Sym3 = Sym9 ⊕ Sym5 ⊕ Sym3 ;
3168   composition_test.py). So closure propagates functorially from the classically nice low pow-
3169   ers Sym2 , Sym3 , Sym4 and from any forcibly-closed fiber to all their composites, tensors, and
3170   base changes. Composition alone — multiplicative top weight 𝑎𝑏 — misses the prime de-
3171   grees, but the tensor is additive: Clebsch–Gordan gives 𝜋 ⊗ Sym𝑟−1 𝜋 = Sym𝑟 ⊕ Sym𝑟−2 , so every
3172   Sym𝑟 is the top block of 𝜋 ⊗ Sym𝑟−1 , its lower block Sym𝑟−2 inductive (composition_test.py).
3173   The whole tower is reachable — there is no degree wall. (The Clebsch–Gordan route con-
3174   trols the standard-𝐿 residual; the cuspidal-twist family a converse theorem consumes closes by
3175   the same channel-agnostic rank-drop, Lemma 59, not a separate input.) Along the induction
3176   the pole is dimensionally clean, Sym𝑟 ⊗𝜏 carrying no trivial constituent for dim 𝜏 < dim Sym𝑟
3177   (TrivialChannel.no_nonzero_hom_of_finrank_lt); and the carrier builds the readout as the
3178   Mellin of an entire theta, not a quotient of 𝐿-functions, so the classical strip-pole obstruction of block
3179   extraction does not arise. The closure is a finite carrier event: the constant mode 𝑅 = lim𝑁 𝐴car (𝑁)/𝑁
3180   of the transported cuspidal fiber, extinguished by the forcible cell closure above (Lemma 61); the
3181   corroborating numerics — native-cell closure 30/30 at the float64 floor on the open Sym5 , Sym13 ,
3182   and the global warped DC |𝐴car |/𝑁 = 3 × 10−4 falling at 𝑁 = 2 × 105 — are calibration (App. B).
3183   Its 1D shadow — the mean of the readout coefficients, equivalently the 𝑠=1 residue — vanishes,
3184   and the tensor structure exhibits why without leaving the carrier: the Clebsch–Gordan factor-
3185   ization 𝐿(𝜋 × Sym𝑟−1 𝜋) = 𝐿(Sym𝑟 𝜋) 𝐿(Sym𝑟−2 𝜋) holds at the coefficient level (verified to 10−14 ,
3186   tensor_induction_check.py), the base GL(2) × GL(𝑟) Rankin–Selberg entire and non-vanishing
3187   at 1, so 𝑅(Sym𝑟 𝜋) = 0 inductively (verified → 0). There is no degree obstruction and no residual
3188   𝑠=1 pole; the 𝑠=1 analysis is the projection’s frame, not the carrier’s, and it too comes out clean.

3189   39 The transported datum: reflection, completion, and niceness laws –
3190      CPS
3191   The candidate object of §37 carries an admissible fiber; Part II here assembles the laws by which the
3192   complete carrier reads it into a faithful completed datum — the local self-duality that certifies the
3193   fiber, the vertical growth of the readout, the carrier reflection and its completion, and the completed
3194   functional equation. These are the supporting laws of the transport machine (Theorem 74). The
3195   automorphic landing they enable — whether the classical automorphic category accepts this output
3196   — is deferred to Part III, where a converse theorem is invoked as an external checksum.
3197       We record the local/analytic ingredients as lemmas, each a proven statement, so the transported
3198   datum is assembled in one place.

3241   For any Rankin–Selberg tensor pair (𝑊𝑟,𝜏 , 𝑊𝑟,𝜏∨ ) harmonization stamps all three: the adapter books the
3242   determinant character (det 𝜑𝜏,𝑣 )𝑟+1 into the warp (F), routes the dual leg on the anti-helix (S), and inherits
3243   the carrier’s ledger positivity (L). So every harmonized CPS twist is admissible: (F) + (S) force 𝑅 + = −𝑅 − ,
3244   whence full focal cancellation drops the Gram rank and the residual direction disappears (Lemma 59), and
3245   (L) makes that a genuine loss of a positive direction, not a cancellation of signed masses. The passport gives
3246   𝑅 𝑟,𝜏 = 0 (no carrier residue) but does not by itself certify pole-freeness of the identified 𝐿-function: a reducible
3247   parameter Sym𝑟 𝜑𝜋 carries a trivial constituent whose 𝜁-factor is a genuine 𝑠 = 1 pole — the classically
3248   enumerated exceptional 𝜋 (§16). Residual extinction is thus a property of every admissible payload; the
3249   intrinsic pole is a property of the reducible parameter alone, and is absent whenever Sym𝑟 𝜑𝜋 is irreducible.
3250   Lemma 64 (Initial convergence and vertical-strip boundedness). For every 1 ≤ 𝑚 < 𝑟 and cuspidal 𝜏
3251   on GL𝑚 , the candidate 𝐿(𝑠, Π𝑟 × 𝜏) converges absolutely in a right half-plane, and its completed Λ(𝑠, Π𝑟 × 𝜏)
3252   is bounded in every vertical strip — as Theorem 39 requires.
3253   Proof. Initial convergence — of the candidate, then the twist. For a cuspidal 𝜋 on GL2 /Q the standard
       bound |𝛼±1         1/2 (Jacquet–Shalika [20], no Ramanujan; any polynomial local bound giving
3254              𝑝 | < 𝑝
3255   some right half-plane would do) gives |𝛼 𝑝𝑟−2𝑘 | < 𝑝 𝑟/2 for the Sym𝑟 weights, so the candidate Euler
3256   product 𝐿(𝑠, Π𝑟 ) converges absolutely on some right half-plane Re 𝑠 > 1 + 2𝑟 . Absolute convergence
3257   of the twist 𝐿(𝑠, Π𝑟 × 𝜏) then follows in some right half-plane by [14, Lemma 2.2] — exactly the
3258   initial-convergence hypothesis of Theorem 39; we do not estimate the Rankin–Selberg coefficients
3259   of every 𝜏 by hand, and Ramanujan is not used. (This reads the deprojected 3D Satake datum with
3260   its radial magnitude, not the 2D unit-circle phase; the sharp 7/64 exponent [16] is available for the
3261   Maass class but is not needed here.) Vertical-strip boundedness, directly from the completed transform.

3275   Theorem 65 (Carrier reflection: the 3D–2D–1D intertwiner). The carrier is a 3D double-ended helix
3276   𝐶 = 𝐶+ ⊔ 𝐶− — helix 𝐶+ and conjugate anti-helix 𝐶− — read through a 2D Cayley/Möbius projection to the
3277   unit-circle chart and a 1D logarithmic readout to the normalized strip. Its completed reflection is generated
3278   geometrically, in dimensional order, for any admissible fiber pair (𝑊 , 𝑊 ∨ ) riding the two lanes:
3279  (J) Global involution. A single symmetry 𝐽 : 𝐶+ ↔ 𝐶− exchanges helix and anti-helix — a geometric
3280      involution of the whole carrier, not a product of local pieces.
3281 (P) Projection intertwines. The Cayley map carries 𝐽 to the unit-circle reflection, 𝜋2D ◦ 𝐽 = 𝐽Cayley ◦ 𝜋2D

3282      (GeometricReadout.cayley, cayley_real_norm_one); the discarded radial and phase coordinates are
3283      booked losslessly — fiber ↦→ (retained height, ledger) is a bĳection (ConeProjection.record_bijective,
3284      reconstruct_record; SourceHolonomy.projection_bijective_loss_ledger).
3285 (C) FE clock intertwines. The functional-equation clock carries the projected reflection to the readout

3286      reflection (FiniteWeightFiber.clockCompletion_selfdual).
3287 (L) Log readout. The logarithm linearizes the multiplicative height, and the unique fixed point of the involution

3288      is the midpoint Re 𝑠 = 12 (ConeProjection.midpoint_to_critical, AutomorphicCandidate.midpoint_projects
3289   Composing, the completed readout obeys Λ(𝑠; 𝑊) = 𝜀𝑊 Λ(1 − 𝑠; 𝑊 ∨ ), |𝜀𝑊 | = 1: the helix reading at 𝑠 is the
3290   anti-helix reading at 1 − 𝑠. The root number 𝜀𝑊 and the conductor are the arithmetic identification of this
3291   geometric reflection — read from the local 𝜀𝑣 (§39.1) — not its definition.

3292   Proof. 𝐽 is the global geometric involution of the double carrier; 𝑧 ↦→ 𝑧¯ about the axis realizes it on
3293   each strand, where the two-strand clock 𝐸𝑣 (𝑧) = 𝑒 𝑖𝑧ℓ𝑣 /2 − 𝛼 𝑣 𝑒 −𝑖𝑧ℓ𝑣 /2 (ChiralityHB.symClock) obeys
3294   the local weld 𝐸𝑣∗ (¯𝑧 ) = − 𝛼¯ 𝑣 𝐸𝑣 (𝑧) (symClock_star) — the readout of 𝐽 at 𝑣, not its definition. Steps (P)
3295   and (L) are the round-trip and midpoint theorems cited; (C) is the completion clock’s self-duality.
3296   The reflection is thus produced by the global carrier and its faithful projection, not assembled
3297   placewise; it yields a unit 𝜂𝑊 with Λ(𝑠; 𝑊) = 𝜂𝑊 Λ(1 − 𝑠; 𝑊 ∨ ), |𝜂𝑊 | = 1 (each geometric clock phase
3298   −¯𝑧 𝑣 having modulus one, 𝑧 𝑣 = 𝛼 𝑣 /|𝛼 𝑣 | the 2D Cayley phase with 𝑧 𝑣 𝑧¯ 𝑣 = 1 — the projected phase,
3299   not the 3D arithmetic Satake parameter 𝛼 𝑣 ). The arithmetic identification 𝜂𝑊 = 𝜀(𝑠, Π𝑟 × 𝜏) with
3300   the standard global root number is a separate computation — from the normalized local 𝜀𝑣 factors
3301   and the conductor (§39.1, (5)), with the usual almost-everywhere product structure — and is not the
3302   bare product of the clock phases − 𝛼¯ 𝑣 , which are the weld’s readout, not the local 𝜀 factor. No lattice
3303   and no Poisson summation enter — the classical theta identity 𝜃(𝑌 −1 ) = det(𝑌)1/2 𝜃(𝑌) of §38 is the
3304   1D readout shadow of 𝐽.                                                                                      □
3305   Formal scope of the concluding identity. The cited Lean intertwiners prove the involution, lossless
3306   coordinate ledger, clock exchange, and logarithmic inversion for a carrier function already obeying
       the exchange law. They do not identify the fixed-kernel global coefficient theta 𝑛 𝜆𝑛 𝑔((𝑛 + 1)𝑥) with
                                                                                               Í
3307

3308   its transformed anti-helix bank for arbitrary Satake coefficients. At the coefficient-theta interface this
3309   distinction is explicit in GlobalHelix.fixedBankOddChannel_eq_zero_iff_theta_reflection:
3310   vanishing of the odd 3D channel is exactly the required global theta reflection, rather than a
3311   consequence of the coordinate involution alone. Consequently the displayed completed-readout
3312   identity applies to the actual twisted 𝐿-function after that odd-channel/global-reflection statement
3313   and the Mellin identification are both supplied.
3314   The unit circle is a projection surface, not a unitarity claim. A point of the 2D chart lies on 𝑆 1 because it is
3315   the phase projection of the source datum 𝛼 = 𝜌 𝑒 𝑖𝜃 ; the radial magnitude 𝜌 is not declared 1 but booked
3316   in the loss ledger and restored at the logarithmic readout (ConeProjection.record_bijective:

                                                              92
3317   fiber ↦→ (height, (radial, phase)) is a bĳection). So 𝛼 = 2 and 𝛼 = 12 ride opposite lanes with
3318   reciprocal radial data and a common unit-circle phase; membership in 𝑆 1 asserts nothing about
3319   |𝛼|. The fiber need not be self-dual. Duality is first a property of the carrier, 𝐶+ ↔ 𝐶− : an admissible
3320   fiber 𝑊 rides one lane while 𝑊 ∨ rides the anti-lane, so a non-self-dual CPS twist is carried by the
3321   pair (𝑊 , 𝑊 ∨ ) and the reflection identifies their readouts at 𝑠 ↔ 1 − 𝑠. What Lemma 62 certifies is
3322   carrier-dual compatibility of the pair, not 𝑊 ≃ 𝑊 ∨ .

3368   Remark 68 (The degree reading of the transfer exponent is a chart statement). Nothing in the carrier
3369   is harder at 𝑟 ≥ 5. Both gates, stated in the 3D chart, are rank-uniform: the per-rail conjugate-pair
3370   reality and det-one ledger are the same finite-multiset algebra at every rank (fiber_det_one,
3371   localPoly_reciprocal — Lean, for any finite duality-stable multiset), and native-cell closure is
3372   the same geometric identity at every rank, measured to 10−𝑝 through GL(14) (§31). What the 1D
3373   chart books as degree-hardness — the Chandrasekharan–Narasimhan exponents, the (𝑑 − 1)/2𝑑
3374   law, the smeared scalar reopening at Sym13 (𝑘 = 0.44, repaired only partially in-chart by the delay
3375   adapter, fully by the channel-resolved readout, §31) — is the same rank-agnostic projection carrying
3376   more channels with a wider spread of spin rates: attrition of the shadow’s bookkeeping, never a
3377   wall of the object. The transfer exponents inherit this. Measured window-drift of the grown slope
3378   (App. B): Δ plateaus (0.040 → 0.000, the proved 𝐴e → 𝐿(0)); Sym5 Δ equilibrates (0.25 → 0.05 in the
3379   late windows — the global 0.29 is a finite-window transient of channel windings not yet averaged);
3380   Sym13 Δ’s fastest channels have not yet equilibrated at 𝑁 = 2 × 105 (late windows oscillatory, no
3381   steady growth). Pre-committed to the falsifiability register: the Sym13 late-window slope falls
3382   with 𝑁 as its channels equilibrate; its persistence at ≈0.46 alongside exact 3D closure would be a
3383   measured chart/carrier divergence, and would be published as such.

3384   Remark 69 (The open inputs live where the ledger is discarded). The descent 3D → 2D → 1D
3385   is not lossy: it is the midpoint/Cayley projection carrying the loss ledger, and the ledgered
3386   map fiber ↦→ (ordinate; radius, angle) is a proven bĳection (ConeProjection.record_bijective,
3387   reconstruct_record — Lean, unconditional; §37). Every input of the niceness chain that the
3388   classical chart still holds open is therefore a statement about the unledgered shadow — the bare
3389   scalar the classical converse theorem consumes after the radius and angle channels are discarded.
3390   The transfer exponent asks whether the bare ordinate coordinate can reach the axis unaided
3391   (“continuation” is the 1D chart’s name for information the ledgered descent preserves trivially: the
3392   bank state exists at every height); axis reality asks whether the bare single-lane readout keeps the
3393   phase lock the ledgered two-lane object has termwise. The latter is now split in Lean at exactly
3394   that seam (RequestProject/AxisPairing.lean): the paired two-lane bank is real termwise on
3395   the axis (pairedBank_real — free, any fiber, no arithmetic); the classical readout decomposes as
3396   (paired + odd)/2 (readout_decomposition); and the axis functional equation is precisely extinction
3397   of the odd lane-mode (fe_iff_oddMode_eq_zero) — the same genre as the residual extinction
3398   𝑅 = 0, where the carrier’s machinery (RequestProject/FocalResidualGeneral.lean, Lemmas 60,
3399   59) is strongest. The frontier is thus not hard analysis at high degree: it is two reach/extinction
3400   statements about a projection that provably discards nothing when its ledger is kept, imposed only
3401   because the classical category reads the unledgered coordinate.

3402   Remark 70 (The two legs are independent). Continuation and axis reality are separate properties
3403   with separate mechanisms, and neither implies the other. Continuation is a scale property: the fiber’s

                                                           94
3404   cells close at its own harmonic scale, the primitive there is bounded, and the readout continues —
3405   presupposing neither the functional equation nor automorphy. Axis reality is a ledger property: the
3406   det-one balance of the completed reflection — a finite non-unimodular cocycle on the reflection
3407   breaks it while leaving closure and continuation intact. The falsification instruments that separate
3408   the two legs empirically are documented in App. B.
       Lemma 71 (Bank reflection: axis reality and continuation). Let 𝐾 𝑟,𝜏 (𝑥) = 𝑛≥1 𝜆𝑛 𝑔(𝑛𝑥) be the

3412   FiniteWeightFiber.fiber_det_one); (ii) the archimedean self-duality 𝛾(𝑠) = 𝜀arch 𝛾(𝜅−𝑠) (FiniteWeightFiber.cloc

3416   Proof. The reflection has two legs — the duality/conjugation leg (𝜏 ↔ 𝜏∨ , the unit 𝜀) and the
3417   height-inversion leg (𝑠 ↦→ 𝜅 − 𝑠) — and the carrier supplies them at different places.
3418        Step 1: on the weld axis, inversion IS conjugation. On Re 𝑠 = 𝜅/2 one has 𝜅 − 𝑠 = 𝑠¯ exactly, so
3419   the height-inversion leg degenerates there to conjugation — the one symmetry the involution
3420   𝐽 implements phasor by phasor (Theorem 65). (As an identity of the 1D analytic readouts
3421   this is consumed only after Step 2 supplies their axis values; on the carrier itself it is chart-
3422   free — the standing wave is read directly at the weld.) With the unitary dual coefficients
3423   𝜆∨𝑛 = 𝜆¯ 𝑛 and the real completion kernel, Λ(𝜅 − 𝑠; 𝜏∨ ) = Λ(𝑠; 𝜏) on the axis, so the claimed
       equation restricted to the axis is exactly 𝜀𝑟,𝜏 Λ( 𝜅2 + 𝑖𝑡; 𝜏) ∈ R — the standing wave: the two-lane

3426   and the self-dual completion clock (ii) (frobeniusBlock_deBranges_reality_bridge per block;
       collapseWave_even, hinge_turning_point at the weld; the ledger unit 𝜀𝑟,𝜏 = 𝑣 𝜀𝑣 , |𝜀𝑟,𝜏 | = 1

3427

3428   from localPoly_reciprocal). The reflection is read where the carrier itself reads it — at the weld
3429   — not reassembled from local data at a convergence edge.
3430        Step 2: continuation carries the axis identity everywhere. Both completed readouts must be
3431   analytic on an open strip containing the axis. A character’s cells close at the base harmonic
3432   scale and its primitive is bounded; the readout continues across the strip, machine-checked
3433   end-to-end (dirichlet_strip_tendsto_LFunction, eta_strip_tendsto). For a general fiber this
3434   step is discharged either by the raw primitive-exponent hypothesis of Lemma 66, or by apply-
3435   ing InverseWarpKernelTransfer.inverseWarp_transfer_tendsto after proving its summable
3436   inverse-kernel difference and vanishing-boundary conditions for the configured warp. The cell-
3437   solvability theorems ForcibleClosure.residual_forcible and CarrierReachability.reachable_independent
3438   do not by themselves prove these analytic conditions. Equivalently, the fixed-completion route
3439   may establish continuation from a reflected rapidly decaying coefficient theta; its initial-half-plane
3440   Mellin identification is the compiled theorem CarrierTheta.theta_hasMellin_of_polynomial,
3441   while the global reflection of that same fixed-kernel theta is the remaining construction. On a
3442   neighbourhood supplied by one of these routes, the two sides of the claimed equation are analytic
3443   and agree on the axis, a set with accumulation points; by the identity theorem they agree identically.
3444   The dependency order is continuation → axis reality → functional equation → theta identity:
3445   with the residual extinct (Lemmas 60, 59) Mellin inversion returns the summed-bank self-duality
3446   𝐾 𝑟,𝜏 (1/𝑥) = 𝜀𝑟,𝜏 𝑥 𝜅 𝐾 𝑟,𝜏∨ (𝑥) as an output, which is what the Riemann–Hecke split of Prop. 55 (E) and
3447   the direct strip bound of Lemma 64 then consume — no step feeds on its successor.

                                                             95
3448       Why no Poisson — and why not termwise. Off the axis, 𝑥 ↦→ 1/𝑥 mixes distinct phasors: the
3449   reciprocal-height identity is a resummation across the bank, and per-phasor symmetry alone cannot
3450   supply it. Classically that resummation is Poisson/modularity — unavailable at 𝑟 ≥ 5. The route
3451   above never performs it: the inversion leg is used only on the axis, where it is conjugation, and
3452   continuation — a carrier property, not the fiber’s automorphy — carries it off. The 1D co-convergence
3453   gap ({Re 𝑠 > 𝜎0 } ∩ {Re 𝑠 < 𝜅 − 𝜎0 } empty for 𝜎0 > 𝜅/2) is the scalar chart’s record of the same
3454   fact: the half-plane series cannot reach the axis, so the classical frame must resummate; the carrier
3455   readout, continued to the axis by cell closure, need not.                                           □
3456   Axis reality is per-block Lean, whole-bank geometric (𝐽 with the balanced ledger), and machine-zero
3457   across the measured suite — Dirichlet Lean-complete, the Siegel (Sp(2𝑔, Z)) and Godement–Jacquet
3458   (GL(𝑟+1, Z)) carrier lattices, the twisted family through Sym13 and 𝐿(Sym5 Δ × 𝐸11 ) (§38, §39.1).

3542   equation is the carrier’s own theta self-duality. We verify this standard-side functional equation
3543   directly beyond the classical range, at Sym5 .

3578   Tate/Godement–Jacquet case, verified numerically at Sym5 . This computation does not itself
3579   address the twisted convolutions 𝐿(𝑠, Sym𝑟 𝜋 × 𝜏); those are treated structurally in Proposition 55
3580   by the reflection of the det-one tensor fiber.

3581   Direct test of the twisted objects. The structural treatment can now be checked head-on
3582   (twisted_cps_instance.py). As a factorizing control, the degree-12 fiber 𝐿(Sym5 Δ × Δ) — built
3583   on the carrier as a genuine twist — reproduces the standard-side product 𝐿(Sym6 Δ) 𝐿(Sym4 Δ)
3584   (Clebsch–Gordan Sym5 ⊗ Sym1 = Sym6 ⊕ Sym4 ) coefficientwise to 1.8 × 10−14 , validating the twisted
3585   pipeline against known quantities. The decisive run is non-factorizing: 𝐿(Sym5 Δ × 𝐸11 ), degree 12
3586   with two independent Satake angles 𝜃Δ , 𝜃𝐸 , does not reduce to symmetric powers of a single form —
3587   the exact shape Theorem 39 consumes past 𝑟 ≤ 4. Its carrier bank has no DC channel (every channel
3588   carries an odd 𝜃Δ -weight, so no total phase is identically zero), and the multi-rail closure tracks
3589   precision (4 × 10−28 at 30 digits, 9 × 10−88 at 90): the residual constant mode vanishes — entireness —
3590   on the twisted family itself, a first direct numerical instance of the converse theorem’s input beyond
3591   the classical range.


3592   40    Generalization: a representation-agnostic transport
3593   The construction is written for Sym𝑟 , but the symmetric-power pattern is nowhere used. This
3594   section isolates what the carrier actually consumes, exhibits the self-duality clock beneath the
3595   functional equation, and states the general transport with its two case-specific inputs.

3596   What the niceness argument uses. Re-read Proposition 55: the reflection pairs a weight channel
3597   𝑤 with its dual −𝑤; the det-one ledger is the balance of the ±𝑤 pairs; the completion is the two-clock
3598   Bessel (4) at the arbitrary shifts |𝑤|; boundedness and continuation are the two outputs of the warped-
3599   Abel representation, and entireness is the Riemann–Hecke continuation of the completed carrier theta
3600   once its finite zero-frequency residual modes are classified and shown to vanish (§39). None mentions
3601   the Chebyshev string {𝑟, 𝑟−2, . . . , −𝑟}. The carrier consumes only a finite weight multiset, its stability
3602   under 𝑤 ↦→ −𝑤, a modulus/determinant ledger, and the local factor det(1−𝑟(𝜑𝑣 (Frob𝑣 ))𝑞 𝑣−𝑠 )−1 . This
3603   is not a heuristic: it is the Lean theorem FiniteWeightFiber.localPoly_reciprocal (§39, App. B),
3604   which proves the ledger and the self-reciprocal local factor — the per-place functional equation
3605   — for any finite duality-stable weight multiset, with Sym𝑟 and Rankin–Selberg as instances. We
3606   also verify it numerically: for the non-Chebyshev Rankin–Selberg weight systems {±(𝑎+𝑏), ±(𝑎−𝑏)}
3607   of 𝐿( 𝑓 × 𝑔) ( 𝑓 , 𝑔 distinct level-one eigenforms; gaps not the uniform 2 of a symmetric power)
3608   the same completion closes the functional equation to machine precision (App. B). The genuine
3609   two-parameter instance 𝐿(Δ × 𝐸11 ) and the self-dual GL(3) = Sym2 of a real (Hejhal-computed)
3610   Maass form are worked in §31: the channel-resolved carrier closes both to precision, while the


                                                           99
3611   collapsed scalar readout degrades for the two-parameter object alone — a projection artifact, not a
3612   property of the fiber (gl4_rankin.py, gl3_maass_selfdual.py). The three-weight clock is not a
3613   new object: it is the two-clock composed with a third, (Bessel𝜇1 ,𝜇2 ) ★M clock𝜇3 , equal to the direct
       3-fold convolution by associativity and with Mellin 𝑖 ΓC (𝑠 + 𝜇𝑖 ) by the convolution theorem
                                                             Î
3614

3615   (App. B); and uniformity is additive, the trace bound ∥clockTraceN∥ ≤ 𝑛 being the sum of the
3616   pairwise two-clock bounds. Everything composes from the two-clock unit.

3617   The self-duality clock. The pairing 𝑤 ↦→ −𝑤, the reflection 𝑠 ↦→ 1 − 𝑠, the conjugation 𝑧 ↦→ 𝑧¯ ,
3618   and the Poisson 𝑆 : 𝜏 ↦→ −1/𝜏 (𝑆2 = −𝐼) are one order-two involution — the self-duality clock, the
3619   𝜇2 generator at scale 𝜋, beneath the 𝜇6 , 𝜇12 weight clocks in the harmonic ladder. Its tick is the
3620   functional equation; its fixed locus is Re 𝑠 = 12 (forced by the area law, scaleBalanced_iff); its
3621   cell is the phase step 𝜋 (the crossing spacing). The weight clocks are the channels it pairs; the
3622   self-duality clock is the pairing. This makes “duality-stable weight multiset” precise — a weight
3623   system closed under the 𝜇2 clock — and, being a structural involution, the clock is Galois-free: that
3624   is exactly why Sym𝑟 , Rankin–Selberg, and the Maass case (Corollary 46) close the same equation
3625   with only the channels changed.

3626   Ramified local data: the filtration tower. The carrier ingests not only the Satake class but the full
3627   Weil–Deligne datum (𝜌, 𝑁) at a ramified place; the raw local character becomes a clock-augmented
3628   local 𝐿- and 𝜀-factor. The monodromy 𝑁 is the 𝔰𝔩2 lowering ladder on the weight string (Steinberg
3629   Sp(𝑛) is the Sym𝑛−1 string with 𝑁 : 𝑤 ↦→ 𝑤 − 2), and 𝐿𝑣 = det(1 − Frob 𝑞 𝑣−𝑠 | (ker 𝑁)𝐼𝑣 )−1 reads
3630   Frobenius on the bottom of each ladder inside the inertia-invariants — as in the twist 𝐿(𝐸, Ad𝑔 ) at
3631   𝑝 = 13, where 𝐸 is Steinberg and the degree drops 2 → 1. The inertia is a root-of-unity clock: tame
                                                                                           𝑎/2
3632   inertia is a 𝜇𝑚 rotation, and the local root number is its Gauss sum 𝜀𝑣 = 𝜏(𝜒)/𝑞 𝑣 (|𝜀𝑣 | = 1, App. B).
3633   Wild inertia is the higher-ramification filtration as a tower 𝜇𝑝 ⊂ 𝜇𝑝 2 ⊂ · · · : the wild 𝜀-factor is the
3634   tower Gauss sum over (Z/𝑝 𝑎 )∗ , and it closes — |𝜀𝑣 | = 1 to 10−15 for conductor 𝑝 𝑎 (𝑎 ≤ 3, Swan ≤ 2),
3635   with the tower’s stationary phase reducing the wild sum to a single tame term keyed by the level-𝑎
3636   character (App. B). So the local dictionary is complete, tame and wild: 𝐿𝑣 from the monodromy
3637   ladder and inertia clock, 𝜀𝑣 from the filtration-tower Gauss sum.

3638   The content: the vanishing-adjustment clock. The layers so far — self-duality, completion,
3639   ramification — are the envelope: shared across a family, carrying no arithmetic. The content is
       a fourth clock. The raw object is the trivial-character series 𝜁(𝑠) = 𝑛 −𝑠 (all channels unit); the
                                                                              Í
3640

3641   Satake/Frobenius datum augments it by setting each phasor’s spin (the phase, the Satake angle
3642   𝜃𝑝 ) and magnitude (|𝑎 𝑛 |, bounded by Ramanujan), continuously in height and stepwise across
3643   primes as the carrier grows. The zeros are the focal cancellation of the adjusted bank — where the
3644   phasors align and sum to zero — located oracle-free by the growth scanner to 10−12 on Dirichlet,
3645   Δ, and 𝐸11 (Appendix B); the root number 𝜀 is the offset at the weld that places or doubles the
3646   central cancellation. Thus the clock-augmented 𝐿-function is the raw 𝜁 carried through four clock
3647   layers: self-duality (the 𝜇2 eta/theta envelope), completion (the two-clock Γ-shape), ramification
3648   (the inertia/monodromy clocks), and this vanishing-adjustment clock (the arithmetic, as phasor
3649   spin and magnitude producing the zeros). The content is not opaque — it is the layer that turns
3650   Satake data into vanishing — though it is fed that data; the clock operates the arithmetic, it does not
3651   conjure it.

3652   The vanishing clock in the Hodge substructure: signature-based cycle detection. The following is
3653   preliminary: a calibration that opened a separate development, the loss-ledger ↔ cycle-filtration correspondence


                                                             100
3654   sketched in §44 and deferred to a companion paper. The completion clock is already the Hodge realization
3655   — ΓC (𝑠 + 𝜇) is the Hodge type (𝑝, 𝑞) with 𝑝 − 𝑞 = 2𝜇 — so the dimension clock projects into a Hodge
3656   structure by construction. Paired with the vanishing clock it reads the algebraic substructure through
3657   the Beilinson–Bloch vanishing–cycle-rank correspondence: in the theorem-anchored instances
3658   below (the identity 𝑟(𝐸, Ad𝑔 ) = rank 𝐸(𝑀) − rank 𝐸(𝑄) of §36.2 and the |Sha| ladder of §37), central
3659   vanishing order agrees with the corresponding cycle multiplicity, while the general correspondence
3660   is deferred to the companion paper; and algebraicity itself is detected by the vanishing signature,
3661   not a single special value. Two instances, both measured (App. B). CM: the (1, 1) class of Sym2 𝐸 is
3662   algebraic iff 𝐸 has complex multiplication, and the clock reads it off the 𝑎 𝑝 -signature — a CM curve
3663   has 𝑎 𝑝 = 0 at every inert prime (399/399 for 𝑦 2 = 𝑥 3 − 𝑥 over Q(𝑖); 4/399 for the non-CM 37𝑎), the
3664   𝜇2 clock of the CM field marking the symmetric-square pole. Twist-correspondence: given 𝑓 and

3668   every 𝜓. The core detection (Rankin–Selberg poles marking twist-equivalence) is classical; what the
3669   clock adds is the unified reading — the vanishing clock’s signature inside the Hodge projection,
3670   one detector — and the dynamical scan that surfaces a correspondence rather than confirming a
3671   known one. Recursive tower: the same signature climbs the symmetric-power tower. The pole order
3672   of 𝐿(Sym𝑟 𝑓 × Sym𝑟 𝑓 ) is the count of algebraic self-correspondences at level 𝑟 — the multiplicity of
3673   the trivial in Sym𝑟 ⊗ Sym𝑟 as a Sato–Tate representation. For a generic form it is 1 at every level
3674   (Sym𝑟 irreducible under SU(2)); for a CM form it climbs 1, 2, 2, 3, · · · = ⌈(𝑟+1)/2⌉, the extra cycles of
3675   𝑁(𝑈(1)) appearing level by level. Measured (App. B): the DC-residue √           slope tower is flat for the
3676   non-CM 37𝑎 and climbs identically for CM over Q(𝑖) and Q( −3), the CM/non-CM ratio tracking
3677   1, 2, 2, 3. The pole orders themselves are the Sato–Tate moments (classical); what the clock supplies
3678   is the recursive reading of the cycle tower, level by level, distinguishing the Sato–Tate/Hodge
3679   structure from the signature alone.

3698   The reflection is carrier geometry; the FE clock adapts it. The functional equation is not an analytic
3699   hypothesis on the fiber but a property of the carrier geometry: the helix–anti-helix conjugation,


                                                           101
3700   fixed at Re 𝑠 = 12 , is the natural functional equation, proven per-place (localPoly_reciprocal) and
3701   invariant under the dual-compatible unit warps (warpFiber). Whether every warp preserves it we
3702   do not assert — and we do not need to, because that is exactly what the FE clock is for. When
3703   the natural reflection already closes (the self-dual, aligned case) the clock is inert. When a warp
3704   perturbs the closure, or when 𝑟 is not self-dual — so the reflection pairs 𝐿(𝑠, 𝑟 ◦ 𝜑) with 𝐿(𝑠, 𝑟 ∨ ◦ 𝜑)
3705   — a tunable FE clock/adapter is switched in to restore it: at its simplest the 𝜇2 self-duality clock
3706   doubling onto 𝑟 ⊕ 𝑟 ∨ , whose weight system {𝑤} ∪ {−𝑤} is closed under 𝑤 ↦→ −𝑤 by construction
3707   so that 𝐿(𝑠, (𝑟 ⊕ 𝑟 ∨ ) ◦ 𝜑) = 𝐿(𝑠, 𝑟 ◦ 𝜑) 𝐿(𝑠, 𝑟 ∨ ◦ 𝜑) carries a genuine self-dual functional equation;
3708   more generally the clock’s phase and scale are tuned to the fiber’s own weight ledger. So the
3709   natural reflection is geometric and free, and FE closure never rests on universal warp-invariance:
3710   the tunable adapter supplies whatever adjustment a given warp requires.

3711   The general transport, and its two inputs. The analytic side is thus representation-agnostic:
3712   functional equation (the carrier reflection), completion (two-clock), and — from the one carrier-cell
3713   theorem (exact zero cell mean of the adapted warp) — continuation, vertical bound, and entireness
3714   hold for every finite duality-stable weight system, uniformly in 𝑟. The transport itself needs nothing
3715   further: it consumes an admissible function — the finite placewise presentation of Definition 5 —
3716   directly, with no local-Langlands datum. Two case-specific steps enter only the classical naming
3717   of the output as 𝑟∗ (𝜋) automorphic on GL𝑁 , neither Sym𝑟 -special: (i) local Langlands for the
3718   source 𝐺 — a translation step, not a system input — to source the admissible presentation from an
3719   automorphic 𝜋 (producing 𝜑𝑣 and the local factors) and to identify the output classically; free for
3720   GL2 (symmetric powers, Rankin–Selberg), a theorem in many cases in general; and (ii) the converse
3721   theorem into GL𝑁 [14], which promotes the nice 𝐿-function to an automorphic form, and whose
3722   twisted-niceness input is again a duality-stable warp the carrier supplies. Within these, Sym𝑟 was
3723   the first nontrivial clock family the carrier consumed, not the mechanism: on the analytic side the
3724   carrier is a representation-agnostic Langlands-transport engine.

3725   Harmonization: the transform dictionary, and the method as its own proof. The whole process
3726   — reading a function, letting its nature name the frame it requires, and enlarging or warping the
3727   carrier to that frame so the function closes — is one we call harmonization, after its classical archetype:
3728   a class-group obstruction is an untranslated frame mismatch that dissolves the moment the carrier
3729   is enlarged to the field the obstruction itself names (capitulation; Furtwängler’s Principal Ideal
3730   Theorem). The function’s nature selects its adapter — one does not pick a universal transform
3731   and hope. And those adapters are, place by place, the established machinery of the Satake–Hecke
3732   picture, re-read. The self-duality clock is the Weyl group acting on the dual torus (for GL(2),
3733   𝛼 ↔ 𝛼−1 ), so a duality-stable weight multiset is a Weyl orbit and the carrier’s duality is built
3734   in; the centering to Re 𝑠 = 12 is the 𝜌-shift 𝛿1/2 ; the completion that assembles the local factor
3735   is Macdonald’s spherical-function formula / the Harish-Chandra 𝑐-function, a Weyl sum over
3736   the orbit; the local factor det(1 − 𝑟(𝐴)𝑞 −𝑠 )−1 is the Satake transform through 𝑟; and the reading
3737   measure is Plancherel. A cuspidal fiber’s function warp is a chart-conversion clock that rationalises
3738   its data: passing from the multiplicative Satake angle to the completely additive prime-count
3739   winding Θ(𝑛) = (𝜋/3)Ω(𝑛) turns the carrier phase into a root of unity 𝛽 Ω(𝑛) (𝛽 = 𝑒 𝑖 𝑘𝜋/3 ) — a
3740   Liouville-type completely multiplicative twist, whatever the (irrational) Satake angle — and the
3741   warp exp(𝑖𝜀 sin 𝑘Θ) is, by Jacobi–Anger, a Bessel-weighted superposition of these root-of-unity
3742   twists (carrier_warp_check.py, carrier_lockin.py), its cell closing by the classical vanishing of
       the Liouville-type mean, 𝑛≤𝑋 𝛽 Ω(𝑛) = 𝑜(𝑋). The claim is in fact universal, only not enumerated:
                                    Í
3743

3744   for every fiber there exists an adapter, selected by the fiber’s own nature, under which it closes —


                                                          102
3745   an ∀∃ statement, not one transform imposed on all — and its archetype, capitulation, is already
3746   a universal theorem (every ideal becomes principal in the frame it names). What we decline is
3747   the enumeration of every (function, adapter) pair. The method is established the way such a
3748   method is: a few representative classes are proved outright (the finite duality-stable harmonic
3749   fibers and the Dirichlet family, in Lean, §39), and a substantial subset of the dictionary is itself
3750   machine-checked rather than merely numerical — the two-clock completion and weight law
3751   (TwoClockWeightLaw: two_clock_weight, ramanujan_line_ceiling, dc_offset), the jet/rank
3752   clock (BSDClocks: rank_is_dc_residue, leading_jet_extraction, gz_first_jet_live), the
3753   arithmetic clock and gauge gap
3754   (ClockStructure: arithmetic_clock_law, gauge_gap_law, obstruction_recovery), the clock–
3755   dip lock-in
3756   (ClockDipDuality: locked_dips_add, unlocked_dips_cancel), the reflection (FiniteWeightFiber),
3757   and the cell closure (CellClosure); the adapters that close the remaining cases are named and
3758   grounded in existing theory (the dictionary above, necessarily partial — some adapters were built
3759   and never needed); and the per-fiber architecture makes the universal principle operative rather
3760   than aspirational — a fiber outside the proved classes engages its own adapter, and a resistant fiber
3761   is diagnostic rather than automatically fatal.
3762       We fully expect novel inputs to expose adapter forms not yet named in the paper. A resistant
3763   fiber either identifies missing structural data in the stated presentation, or exhibits failure of the
3764   synthesized carrier-closure condition; in the latter case it is a counterexample to universality on
3765   the declared source class. This fixes what a genuine counterexample must be. It is not enough
3766   to exhibit a fiber that the present dictionary does not close; a real counterexample must exhibit
3767   a payload for which no harmonization consistent with its intrinsic dynamics can satisfy the carrier and
3768   ledger laws while preserving faithful readout. That is the falsifiable content of the universal claim, and it
3769   is the burden a disconfirmation must meet.

3770   The operational adapter suite. The dictionary above is place-by-place; what operates it is a suite of
3771   three adapters, each keyed to the measured transport clock, that the carrier switches in to close a
3772   readout the raw projection smears (introduced in §30; named here as a unit).
3773 (1) The clock configurator reads the deterministic transport frequency 𝜈clock = 2𝜈𝐽 off the orbital
3774     transform (𝑅2 = 1.000, §30) and sets the period, phase, and scale the other three inherit. It repairs
3775     nothing itself — it configures: identifying the clock is necessary but not sufficient.
3776 (2) The carrier dwell re-registers the values a projected sum skips — the fiber takes a siding whose

3777     length is the height offset, traverses the omitted lattice points, and returns to the same carrier
3778     position with its phasors re-aligned. This is the native, exact form of Altuğ’s Σ() missing-lattice-
3779     point correction (3400× closure contrast against the cut track, §31, skip_insert_closure.py).
                                                                             2       1
3780 (3) The phasor delay adapter, derived from the clock (slope 𝑏 = −1/𝑥 , 𝑥 0 =
                                                                             0       2 log 𝑁, not fit), retards
3781     the faster-spinning higher-weight channels so a single-rail Chebyshev bank does not over-rotate
3782     within a dwell period. On the Sym𝑟 tower it raises the reopening exponent partially (𝑘 : 0.48 → 0.61
3783     at 𝑟 = 13 in the delay experiment dwell_retard.py, whose 0.48 baseline is that experiment’s
3784     setup, distinct from the 0.44 full-readout smear of the §31 table); a single delay is a one-rail
3785     correction, and a genuinely multi-parameter fiber is closed instead by the channel-resolved
3786     (multi-rail) readout of §31, not by a scalar delay.
3787   The clock configurator selects; the other three execute — period, registration, spin, dissipation.
3788   This is the operational face of harmonization: the fiber’s nature, read through the clock, names the
3789   adapters it needs.

3790   41    The transport machine and universal carrier transport
3791   Exotic adapters: the parallel-dimension clock. The clocks above act on one carrier. A transfer
3792   between two automorphic worlds — a functorial lift 𝑟 : 𝐿 𝐺 → 𝐿 𝐻, a theta correspondence, a base
3793   change — is, in this language, a parallel-dimension clock: it absorbs the local state on the source
3794   carrier, reflects it onto an alternate carrier (the target 𝐿 𝐻, or an auxiliary object such as the Weil
3795   representation or an Eisenstein series) that runs its own clock system, applies the transfer there, and
3796   reflects the result back. The archetype is the theta correspondence, where the Weil representation
3797   on the metaplectic cover is such an alternate helix, and the GSp(4) ↔ GL(4) lacing of §38 is one
3798   instance already used. A non-theta instance goes through uniformly on the carrier: quadratic base
3799   change Δ ↦→ Δ𝐸 over 𝐸 = Q(𝑖) — reflect Δ onto the carrier over 𝐸 (the base-change Satake: split
3800   𝑝 giving two channels, inert 𝑝 the Frobenius-squared channel) and reflect back through the 𝜒−4
3801   clock, the factorization 𝐿(Δ𝐸 , 𝑠) = 𝐿(Δ, 𝑠)𝐿(Δ ⊗ 𝜒−4 , 𝑠) — reproduces the base-change Satake exactly
3802   and closes the reflected degree-four functional equation on the equal-shift two-clock 𝐾0 to 10−26
3803   (App. B). Because the alternate carrier may itself carry parallel-dimension clocks, the construction is
3804   recursive — the functoriality web as a tower of reflections. The mechanism is thus not a metaphor:
3805   base change (reducible), Sym𝑟 (irreducible), and theta (dual pair) are three worked instances.
3806   Isolation note. The universal transport arrows consumed below are isolated in Part I: car-
3807   rier/involution in §2, residual dictionary in §7, readout and reflection in §7, and coherent composition
3808   in §8. The theorem below keeps the transported Satake/tensor specialization.

3840   convergence domain, a half-plane Re 𝑠 > 𝜎0 on which the product converges absolutely. These four data are
3841   a finite structural presentation: 𝑊 is named by finitely much information per place and one bounded-degree
3842   rule, not by its values. The placewise assignment 𝑣 ↦→ 𝐴𝑣 (𝑊) is required to be generated by a finite rule —
3843   a finite parameter set or effective structural schema fixed independently of how many places are queried, not a

3845   not merely finite local dimension at each place. A source carrying no such law — a structureless (“random”)
3846   function whose only faithful description is its own sample path — is not admissible: there is no finite structure
3847   from which to synthesize a carrier phase, a native cell, or a clock, and letting an adapter encode the sample
3848   path would be oracular and vacuous. Admissibility is exactly finite structural presentation. No functional
3849   equation, continuation, entireness, boundedness, or Ramanujan bound is assumed. Then 𝑊 admits
3850   a faithful carrier representation — a carrier encoding the local inputs (i)–(ii), a fiber encoding the function
