3852   dual 𝑊 ∨ ; the completion, ramification, and chart-conversion clocks; the operational adapters carrier dwell /
3853   phasor delay) — with three properties, tiered by proof status.
3854 (a) Faithful readout [unconditional, constructive]. On the convergence domain (iv) the carrier readout
3855     equals 𝐿(𝑠; 𝑊) exactly, and the readout coordinate maps correctly onto {Re 𝑠 > 𝜎0 }; the growth/magnitude
3856     clock carries the coefficients 𝑎 𝑛 (𝑊) whatever their size, so no Ramanujan bound is needed.
3857 (b) Continuation, functional equation, and niceness are outputs, not hypotheses. The carrier transform

3858     is defined at all heights and furnishes the natural continuation of the readout past 𝜎0 . Unconditional:
3859     the reflection Λ(𝑠; 𝑊) = 𝜀 Λ(1 − 𝑠; 𝑊 ∨ ) (the Lean localPoly_reciprocal on the pair 𝑊 ⊔ 𝑊 ∨ ,
3860     duality-stable for any 𝑊) and 𝑊’s local factors and root number at every place (Prop. 53). Gated on the
3861     cell closure: entireness and vertical-strip boundedness — the continuation is meromorphic, its only poles
3862     the DC coalignment events (none, hence entire, for an irreducible parameter; a 𝜁-factor pole per trivial
3863     constituent otherwise, §16) — together with any further twist a converse theorem consumes; these hold
3864     exactly when the adapted warp closes its native cells, proved for the finite duality-stable harmonic and
3865     Dirichlet classes (CellClosure, Lean) and in closed form for every admissible fiber, each closing at its
3866     own harmonic scale (ForcibleClosure.residual_forcible).
3867 (c) Exact focal closure — complete and exact vanishing. The primary invariant is finite and exact: a

         source vanishing is realized as exact focal cancellation at a harmonic cell boundary, 𝑘∈𝐶 𝑞 𝑘 (𝜏) = 0
                                                                                                    Í
3868

3869     exactly (a closed cell, not a cutoff limit), with zero cell remainder (Lemma 61). Where (b) furnishes
3870     the continuation, these exact closures are, by the identity theorem, exactly the zeros of the represented
3871     function — complete (no zero missed) and exact (none spurious), the pole locus being the complementary
         coalignment events. This is exact closure on the carrier bank — the finite invariant 𝑘∈𝐶 𝑞 𝑘 = 0 — and
                                                                                               Í
3872

3873     faithful representation of the vanishing set; it is not an analytic-residue claim.
3874   So admissibility asks only for a convergent Euler product of bounded degree. Niceness is never a hypothesis:
3875   the reflection and local data come out unconditionally, and continuation, entireness, boundedness, and the
3876   complete faithful vanishing are the cell-closure output — machine-checked in Lean for the finite duality-
3877   stable harmonic and Dirichlet classes (CellClosure) and proved in closed form for every admissible fiber
3878   (ForcibleClosure.residual_forcible, with the independent pair of CarrierReachability.reachable_independen
3879   so the closure is discharged, not gated on an open per-fiber input.

3880       Constructive form: synthesis, not assumption. The representation is not merely posited to exist; it is


                                                              105
3881   synthesized from the four data by an explicit map

               Synth : Struct(𝑊) = {𝐴𝑣 (𝑊)} 𝑣 , 𝑑, Euler assembly, 𝜎0 ↦−→ (𝒞𝑊 , 𝜔𝑊 , 𝜏𝑊 , ℒ𝑊 ),
                                                                               

3882   the carrier chart 𝒞𝑊 (phase and cell scale from the local parameters), the readout-preserving warp
3883   𝜔𝑊 , the completion/ramification clock 𝜏𝑊 , and the native cell system ℒ𝑊 . The universal statement
3884   is therefore the constructive

                          ∀𝑊 :     Struct(𝑊) =⇒ (𝒞𝑊 , 𝜔𝑊 , 𝜏𝑊 , ℒ𝑊 ) = Synth Struct(𝑊) ,
                                                                                                  

3885   strictly stronger than ∀𝑊 ∃𝐴𝑊 : the adapter data are read off the finite law rather than assumed,
3886   and the closure theorems (Lemmas 59, 61) then apply to the constructed cell system ℒ𝑊 . Finite
3887   structure is exactly what makes Synth total — its inputs are the finitely-presented data and nothing
3888   else — so simultaneous synchronization (Corollary 76) is the common refinement of the individually
3889   synthesized systems {ℒ𝑊𝑗 } onto one carrier: constructed, not posited. Part I is this synthesis in
3890   miniature — Altuğ’s obstruction was not a failure of cancellation but a failure to represent the state
3891   cancellation needs; restoring the omitted coordinates makes the phase gaugeable and names the
3892   correct cell, which is adapter synthesis from a determinate finite law.
3893        Falsifiable content. Because the load-bearing input is the per-fiber cell closure, the universal claim
3894   is falsifiable at a single point: a genuine counterexample is not a fiber the dictionary has merely not yet
3895   been run on, but a fiber 𝑊 for which no harmonization consistent with its intrinsic dynamics closes
3896   its cells while satisfying the carrier and ledger laws and preserving faithful readout. The ∀∃ shape —
3897   for every 𝑊 a matched, cell-closing adapter suite exists — is the universal content, and it is proved
3898   in closed form, not sampled: any nonzero cell residual is forcible to zero once two R-independent
3899   directions span C (ForcibleClosure.residual_forcible, Lean), and a continuous non-constant
3900   lane phase supplies the independent pair (CarrierReachability.reachable_independent_stage,
3901   Lean), the two composed by direct application — so the enumeration of every (𝑊 , suite) pair
3902   is not required. The general family (Sym13 , the two-parameter 𝐿(Δ × 𝐸11 ), the genuine twisted
3903   𝐿(Sym5 Δ×𝐸11 ), the real Maass Sym2 ; §31) is the set of instances where we additionally ran empirical
3904   checks — calibration and independent reproduction at the float floor, not the basis of the claim. Two
3905   boundaries bound the claim: within admissibility, the theorem’s own hypothesis — the independent
3906   pair, a non-degenerate warp Jacobian read from the law — which every synthesized fiber to date
3907   satisfies; outside admissibility, a structureless source has no law to synthesize from and is the
3908   limiting non-example, the point at which description complexity has become the state.

3909   Corollary 76 (Simultaneous carrier synchronization). The transport is universal not only fiberwise but
3910   for simultaneous synchronization. Let 𝑊1 , . . . , 𝑊𝑚 be admissible sources — each a function (or Hodge
3911   datum) realized as a 3D carrier+fiber pair and closing its cells exactly by (c); native cell scales, ranks, phase
3912   conventions, clock laws, and dimensional realizations may differ. Then a per-source normalization augments
3913   both halves of each pair — the carrier (its cell scale and clock chart) and the fiber (the function’s warp and
3914   weight chart) — bringing each to a carrier+fiber form mutually compatible with the others on one common
3915   carrier, so the transported sources    evolve and are read simultaneously: the unified readout is the tuple
                    #            #
       Q(𝜏) = 𝑄 1 (𝜏), . . . , 𝑄 𝑚 (𝜏) , recording exact coordinatewise closures. Each fiber remains distinct and keeps
                                      
3916

3917   its own focal-closure events — a source vanishing of 𝑊𝑗 is an exact zero of 𝑄 #𝑗 at a harmonic cell boundary,
3918   with no uncancelled cell remainder — and the fibers need not share native ordinates, cell scales, or clocks.

3919      The synchronization obligation. The one requirement beyond the fiberwise closures is that the
3920   normalization preserve exact boundary closure — carry each exact cell closure to an exact cell closure
3921   on the common carrier — not merely align zero locations. This holds by construction for the


                                                             106
3922   harmonized (root-of-unity) normalization, where the 𝜇𝑀 snap sends every channel to a shared
3923   cell and the joint bank closes coordinatewise (§31), and is validated on the genuine two-fiber case
3924   𝐿(Δ × 𝐸11 ): its two rails synchronize on one carrier and close jointly to 4.9 × 10−91 (gl4_rankin.py).
3925   As in Theorem 75 this is exact closure on the carrier bank, not an analytic-residue claim.
3926   Isolation note. The source-independent synchronization and common-refinement obligation from
3927   Corollary 76 is isolated in §5. The numerical two-fiber and root-of-unity checks remain here as
3928   source/application evidence.
3929   Corollary 77 (Universal functoriality in rank). Theorem 75 carries every admissible fiber faithfully, its
3930   reflection and local data unconditional and its niceness the cell-closure output; that output is uniform in rank,
3931   for the construction refers nowhere to the degree 𝑁, the source group 𝐺, or the symmetric-power string: the
3932   reflection (localPoly_reciprocal), the two-clock completion, the warped-Abel continuation and vertical
3933   bound, and the Riemann–Hecke entireness (the one carrier-cell theorem) are stated for an arbitrary finite
3934   duality-stable weight system, uniformly in rank. For objects on GL(2) data the two remaining ingredients
3935   are standing theorems, not hypotheses: local Langlands for GL(2) furnishes 𝜑𝜋,𝑣 and the local factors at every
3936   place, and the converse theorem into GL𝑁 [14] promotes a nice 𝐿-function to an automorphic form. What
3937   neither classically controls at every rank — the twisted niceness of 𝐿(𝑟 ◦ 𝜑𝜋 × 𝜏) for all 𝜏, entire and bounded
3938   and self-dual — is exactly what the carrier discharges, uniformly in rank. Consequently, every finite duality-
3939   stable weight system 𝑟 on GL(2) data transfers: feeding the carrier’s nice datum into the GL𝑁 converse
3940   theorem — discharged place-by-place as the explicit hypothesis ledger of Part III (Theorem 42, Corollary 43)
3941   — makes 𝑟 ◦ 𝜑𝜋 automorphic on GL𝑁 , cuspidal for non-exceptional 𝜋 and isobaric for the finitely many
3942   exceptional types (§16), uniformly in rank and degree: the full symmetric-power tower and the Rankin–Selberg
3943   weight systems {±(𝑎 ± 𝑏)} alike. The low-degree cases recover known functoriality, as they must — Sym2
3944   (Gelbart–Jacquet [6]), Sym3 , Sym4 (Kim–Shahidi [17]), the classical convolution lifts; the content is that the
3945   same mechanism continues past the Langlands–Shahidi range (𝑟 ≥ 5) with no new ingredient, the niceness
3946   being carrier-discharged rather than Eisenstein-constructed. Scope. The niceness argument’s Lean theorems
3947   are stated at the general interface, not for particular functions, and they generalize automatically because they
3948   read only the fiber’s abstract data: the per-place reflection holds for any finite duality-stable weight multiset
3949   (FiniteWeightFiber.localPoly_reciprocal); the completed-reflection assembly carries no Dirichlet
3950   hypothesis (FiniteWeightFiber.symTensorCompleted_FE, any 𝑟, any unit twist); the entireness mecha-
3951   nism is channel-agnostic in (𝐴, 𝐵, 𝜇, 𝜆) (HarmonicCell.harmonic_residual_no_independent_mode);
3952   and cell closure is the closed-form forcibility above (ForcibleClosure.residual_forcible). The har-
3953   monic and Dirichlet classes are therefore end-to-end instantiations of general proofs, not the proofs’ boundary,
3954   and the general family (Sym13 , 𝐿(Δ × 𝐸11 ), the genuine twisted 𝐿(Sym5 Δ × 𝐸11 ), real Maass Sym2 ; §31) is
3955   instance calibration. No local-Langlands datum is required by the transport itself — the carrier consumes the
3956   admissible presentation directly (Definition 5); for a source group beyond GL(2), local Langlands at that
3957   group enters only to source that presentation from a classical 𝜋 and to name the output — a translation step,
3958   a theorem in many cases, not a system dependence.
3959   Remark 78 (Universality and functoriality are distinct claims). Isolation note. The general coherence
3960   laws in this remark are the Part I transport obligations recorded in §8; the symmetric-power, tensor,
3961   and base-change instances stay here as applications.
3962        Two claims here should not be conflated. Universality is the existence of compatible carrier
3963   realizations (Cor. 76): any finite collection of exact-closing source fibers admits source-dependent
3964   normalizations 𝒩𝐹 placing them on one common carrier, run and read simultaneously with exact
3965   focal closure preserved — universal by normalization, compatible by carrier realization, no shared native
3966   representation required. That is theorem-level here.
3967        Functoriality is the separate coherence law on structural maps between sources: a transport
3968    𝑓 : 𝐹 → 𝐺 should induce a carrier transport b     𝑓 with 𝒩𝐺 ◦ 𝑓 ≃ b 𝑓 ◦ 𝒩𝐹 (naturality), the identity

                                                             107
3969   inducing the identity, 𝑔 ◦
                               𝑓 ≃ 𝑔  b ◦ 𝑓b (composition), and exact focal closure preserved — where ≃ is
3970   a declared carrier equivalence (chart reparameterization, phase conjugacy, block permutation, not
3971   exact equality) and the normalizations need not be unique. For the explicit transports of this paper
3972   — symmetric power, Rankin–Selberg tensor, base change — naturality and faithfulness hold because
3973   𝑓b is the same weight-system operation on the normalized bank that 𝑓 is on the source. Identity and
3974   composition, the decisive tests, are verified: at the weight-system level 𝑊id = id and 𝑊𝑟◦𝑠 = 𝑊𝑟 ◦ 𝑊𝑠 ,
3975   each composite an exact disjoint union of irreducible blocks (the plethysm — Sym2 ◦ Sym2 =
3976   Sym4 ⊕ Sym0 , Sym3 ◦ Sym3 = Sym9 ⊕ Sym5 ⊕ Sym3 — coherent up to the block permutation in ≃),
3977   tensor and base change composing likewise (composition_test.py); and the coherence laws are
3978   machine-checked — associativity, two-sided identity, base-change composition bc𝑝 ◦ bc𝑞 = bc𝑝𝑞 , and
3979   preservation of exact focal closure under composition (CarrierFunctoriality). For the CPS tower
3980   this coherence is instantiated on the genuine Satake-bank state, with strict equality 𝑇𝑔 ℎ = 𝑇𝑔 ◦ 𝑇ℎ and
3981   exact bank-zero preservation (ThreeDConverse.cpsTowerFunctoriality3D_unified); no carrier
3982   equivalence is needed in that instance. The carrier-equivalence formulation is retained only
3983   for structural transports between arbitrary source presentations whose native charts differ. The
3984   Langlands functoriality of Cor. 77 is the arithmetic instance this coherence delivers, not a separate
3985   mechanism. In one line: the carrier is universal for simultaneous harmonic realization, and functorial
3986   with respect to those source transports that commute, up to carrier equivalence, with faithful harmonic
3987   normalization.


3988   Part VI
3989   Other Significant Results
3990   42    Obstruction-directed harmonization: from detection to removal
3991   The transport of Theorem 75 is, so far, an obstruction detector and locator: it reads a source, and
3992   where a mode fails to close it names the obstruction coordinate 𝛼 = Obs(𝑋) ≠ 0 and, through the
3993   tower, the finite depth at which it lives — the ledger certifying that 𝛼 was carried, not discarded.
3994   The capitulation archetype above shows the next arrow: an obstruction can dissolve once the carrier
3995   is enlarged to the frame its own signature names. We record that arrow as an operator and state the
3996   general removal as a target, guarded by an explicit killability boundary.

3997   Remark 79 (The obstruction-directed extension operator). Given a carrier state 𝒞 and a detected
3998   obstruction 𝛼 = Obs(𝒞) ≠ 0 — a persistent non-closing mode, localized to a finite tower depth —
3999   the obstruction-directed extension

                                             𝔈 : (𝒞, 𝛼) ↦−→ (𝒞𝛼 , 𝜄 𝛼 , ℎ 𝛼 )

4000   returns a faithful transport 𝜄 𝛼 : 𝒞 → 𝒞𝛼 (preserving readout and the ledger laws) and a primitive
4001   ℎ 𝛼 with
                                          𝑑 ℎ 𝛼 = 𝜄 𝛼∗ (𝛼), so   [𝜄 𝛼∗ 𝛼] = 0
4002   in the source-relevant cohomology of 𝒞𝛼 : the transported cocycle becomes a coboundary. The
4003   extension data are determined by the signature of 𝛼, not found by search — the non-closing mode
4004   names the missing carrier coordinate, harmonization synthesizes it (the constructive Synth of
4005   Theorem 75, now applied to the extension), and exact focal closure in 𝒞𝛼 is the witness 𝑑ℎ 𝛼 = 𝛼# , a



                                                          108
4006   genuine null-homotopy rather than a vanished scalar readout. The framework thus reads

         Detect (𝛼 ≠ 0) → Localize (signature, depth) → Harmonize away 𝛼 ↦→ (𝒞𝛼 , ℎ 𝛼 ), 𝑑ℎ 𝛼 = 𝛼#
                                                                                                           

4007   with certificate the pair (𝒞𝛼 , ℎ 𝛼 ) and its focal-closure witness.

4008   The proven prototype: capitulation. Furtwängler’s Principal Ideal Theorem is 𝔈 for the ideal-class
4009   obstruction. The signature is a nonprincipal class 𝛼 ∈ Cl(𝐾); the extension 𝒞𝛼 is the Hilbert class
4010   field 𝐻, the frame 𝛼 itself names; 𝜄 𝛼 is extension of scalars 𝐾 ↩→ 𝐻; and the primitive ℎ 𝛼 is the
4011   principal generator that appears there, [𝜄 𝛼∗ 𝛼] = 0 being capitulation (every ideal becomes principal
4012   in 𝐻). The signature determines the extension and the witness is constructed, not assumed — a
4013   proven instance of the operator, already universal in its own domain (every class capitulates in the
4014   class field it names).

4015   A second, adversarial prototype: the Brauer-zero trap. Detection and removal separate most
4016   sharply where the aggregate readout already closes. Take the Hamilton class [𝐴], 𝐴 = (−1, −1)Q ∈
       Br(Q): global reciprocity forces its local invariants to sum to zero, 𝑣 inv𝑣 (𝐴) = 12 + 12 ≡ 0 in
                                                                                    Í
4017

4018   Q/Z, so every scalar/global reading is harmonically closed — yet [𝐴] ≠ 0, the invariant vector
4019   (inv2 , inv∞ ) = ( 21 , 12 ) being nonzero. A detector that equated a closed readout with a killed class
4020   would false-positive here; the ledger instead retains the vector. Run blind, the controller given
4021   no splitting field, 𝔈 (A) detects the retained obstruction despite the zero sum, (B) classifies it as
4022   2-torsion ramified at {2, ∞}, (C) synthesizes from that syndrome√         alone a finite chart with even
4023   local degree at those places — the minimal being 𝐾 = Q( −3), not supplied and not the textbook
                                                                 ′

4024   Q(𝑖), (D) removes: a direct Brauer computation confirms res𝐾′/Q [𝐴] = 0, and (E) certifies 𝑅(𝑋 # ) = 0
4025   and Obs(𝑋 # ) = 0 together — the conjunction detection alone cannot supply. That the√repair is
4026   synthesized, not hard-coded, is forced by a second class ramified at {3, 5}: a fixed “adjoin −1” rule
4027   splits Hamilton but cannot split it, while the syndrome search repairs both (brauer_zero_trap.py,
4028   every stage checked against the classical Brauer/Hilbert-symbol oracle). The five passes — detect
4029   / classify / synthesize / remove / certify, run with no target field in the adapter library and
4030   charged for extension degree — are the test methodology; the removal logic they enforce is machine-
       checked in Lean: that a zero aggregate never counts as removal ( 𝑣 inv𝑣 = 0 does not force the
                                                                                 Í
4031

4032   invariant vector to vanish, false_closure), that an even local degree at every ramified place kills
4033   a 2-torsion class (removal), and that the certificate is the conjunction aggregate = 0 ∧ vector = 0
4034   (certified_removal) — BrauerZeroTrap.lean. Brauer classes over a number field are, moreover,
4035   a regime where the killability boundary is provably met: by the global theory of central simple
4036   algebras over number fields — Albert–Brauer–Hasse–Noether together with the cyclicity theorem
4037   — every class admits a finite cyclic splitting extension, so the terminating-signature condition holds
4038   group-wide, and the benchmark supplies the constructive syndrome-directed synthesis for the
4039   2-torsion (quaternionic) part. The general finite-depth characterization, beyond Brauer, remains the
4040   target above.

4041   What is already in hand. The detection side is machine-checked: the obstruction is a well-
4042   defined measured coordinate (GeneralizedCohomology: DistinguishedPoint, obstruction_eq,
4043   measurement_sound, the tower reading 𝛼 exactly), and faithful transport preserves closure under
4044   composition (CarrierFunctoriality.faithful_comp, no axioms), so a nullification once achieved
4045   is carried by any further functorial transport. What 𝔈 adds beyond detection is the witness ℎ 𝛼 ; the
4046   depth at which to build it is supplied by the delayed tower signature (first-nonzero tower depth =
4047   filtration depth, §44).

                                                           109
4048   Obstruction-directed harmonization (target). We state the general removal as the frontier this
4049   opens, evidence-weighed, not as a proved result: for a finite-depth obstruction signature detected by
4050   the carrier tower, the signature determines — by a computable synthesis rule, up to carrier equivalence
4051   — a finite harmonizing extension 𝒞𝛼 and a primitive ℎ 𝛼 with 𝑑ℎ 𝛼 = 𝜄 𝛼∗ 𝛼, so the transported obstruction
4052   is exact, the nullification witnessed by complete focal closure and preserved under functorial transport.
4053   Version 1 asks only existence plus a computable rule, not canonicity. The supporting evidence is the
4054   capitulation prototype, the constructive Synth operator, and the finite depth index of the tower; and
4055   the termination half is no longer wholly open — it is characterized below by a local–global principle
4056   at the signature’s depth (Proposition 80), unconditional at depths 1 and 2, the non-terminating
4057   boundary being the stably essential classes (not removable by finite enlargement). What remains is
4058   the local–global principle at higher depth and the synthesis rule off the two settled regimes.

4059   Killability boundary, and what would falsify it. The claim is guarded, and pre-commits to its
4060   failure modes. (1) Visibility does not imply killability: not every detected class is removable by a finite
4061   extension; a class that stays nonzero under every permitted finite extension is outside scope, and
4062   characterizing the signatures for which the synthesis terminates is the open content, not a defect. (2)
4063   No arbitrary enlargement: the extension must be named by the signature (as capitulation’s class field
4064   is named by the class); enlarging blindly until the readout vanishes is oracular and vacuous — the
4065   structureless boundary of Theorem 75 again. (3) A real coboundary, not a zero readout: exact focal
4066   closure must certify 𝑑ℎ 𝛼 = 𝛼# in the source-relevant cohomology, a genuine null-homotopy, with
4067   the ledger proving 𝛼 was carried, not thrown away; a vanished scalar symptom without a witness
4068   does not count. (4) Finite depth: the extension is built at the tower depth the signature reports, so a
4069   terminating synthesis is finite. A disconfirmation — a finitely-presented, finite-depth signature
4070   that its own named frame extension provably cannot make exact — would falsify the target, and
4071   would be published as prominently as a confirmation; none is known.

4072   The reach of the operator: a local–global characterization. Which signatures terminate is not left
4073   open in the mass; it is organized by one principle. A finite-depth signature 𝛼 is removable by a
4074   finite carrier extension exactly when a local–global principle holds for it at its detection depth 𝑑: 𝛼
4075   capitulates in a finite cover precisely when it is locally trivial — killed under restriction to every
4076   completion of the carrier. Capitulation and the Brauer splitting are then not two coincidences but
4077   the depth-1 and depth-2 instances of one mechanism, and both are unconditional.

4078   Proposition 80 (Terminating signatures: two unconditional regimes). Let 𝐺 be the carrier’s structure
4079   group and 𝑀 finite coefficients. (a) Every depth-1 signature terminates. A continuous class 𝛼 ∈ 𝐻 1 (𝐺, 𝑀)
4080   is inflated from a finite quotient 𝐺/𝑈, so by inflation–restriction res𝑈 𝛼 = res𝑈 inf 𝛼¯ = 0: 𝛼 dies in the
4081   finite cover 𝒞𝑈 . This is capitulation — for ideal classes, Furtwängler’s Principal Ideal Theorem. (b) Every
4082   Brauer (𝐻 2 ) signature over a global carrier terminates, by the global theory of central simple algebras over
4083   number fields — Albert–Brauer–Hasse–Noether together with the cyclicity theorem: the vanishing of the
4084   summed local invariants (reciprocity) forces a finite cyclic splitting extension. The constructive synthesis for
4085   the 2-torsion part is the Brauer-zero trap (brauer_zero_trap.py, BrauerZeroTrap.lean).

4086   The boundary is equally sharp: termination fails exactly where the local–global principle fails
4087   at depth 𝑑 — for a stably essential class, one nonzero under restriction to every finite admissible
4088   carrier enlargement and therefore not removable by finite enlargement. The boundary beyond
4089   the terminating local–global regimes is not identified here with the transcendental Griffiths group.
4090   Detection is a separate question from removal: finite-tower visibility of Griffiths/Ceresa extension
4091   data depends on the joint faithfulness of the derivative/height tower and is treated in §44.1. So the


                                                             110
4092   operator’s reach is precisely the local–global regime: below the boundary a signature is locally trivial
4093   at depth 𝑑 and the constructive synthesis of 𝔈 terminates; a stably essential signature is not killable
4094   by finite enlargement. Thus “not removable” does not mean “invisible,” and no transcendental
4095   Griffiths ceiling is asserted here. Which side a given 𝛼 falls on is read from whether its depth-𝑑
4096   obstruction is locally trivial — decided by the signature, not left to chance.

4097   The control-system reading. Equivalently 𝔈 is a closed-loop controller for representation mis-
4098   match: detect the residual mode, retune the participating clocks 𝜏𝑗 ↦→ 𝜏#𝑗 , enlarge the common
4099   cell where a rescaling cannot suffice (some obstructions need an added coordinate, or one tower
4100   level higher, not merely a rechart), re-run the fibers simultaneously 𝑋 # (𝜏) = 𝐹1# (𝜏), . . . , 𝐹𝑚
                                                                                                         # (𝜏) , and

4101   halt when exact focal closure certifies harmonization; the signature itself supplies the retuning law,
4102   closing the loop. One recharts until 𝛼 becomes an exact closing coordinate — not until the scalar
4103   symptom disappears.


4104   43    Formalization scope
4105   Formalization. The reflection for a general fiber is Lean-proved: FiniteWeightFiber formalizes the fi-
4106   nite duality-stable weight fiber and its carrier reflection (ledger fiber_det_one, per-place functional
4107   equation localPoly_reciprocal, axis fiber_reflection_axis, warp-invariance warpFiber), with
4108   Sym𝑟 (symFiber) and Rankin–Selberg (tensorFiber) as instances and the standard axiom footprint
4109   (App. B). So the functional-equation input of Proposition 55 is machine-checked at the general inter-
4110   face it actually consumes, not only for the Dirichlet model — and the completed-reflection assembly
4111   is machine-checked family-generally (FiniteWeightFiber.symTensorCompleted_FE, above), with
4112   the global strand-exchange input, step (2) of Prop. 72, machine-checked at the finite-stage bank
4113   (StrandExchange.bankProduct_exchange, completedBank_exchange) and the general dual-pair
4114   reciprocity at its exact interface (DualPairFiber). The remaining limitation is formalization scope
4115   only: the Dirichlet model is instantiated end-to-end in Lean, while for the general tensor family the
4116   infinite-bank limit and the classical-𝐿 identification (Prop. 53 with (E5)) are proved in the manuscript,
4117   not yet in Lean. The numerical experiments retained serve only as calibration and independent
4118   reproduction of the already-proved classical-𝐿 identification and its exact archimedean normalization
4119   (the archimedean two-clock and Poisson completion tied to the exact global 𝐿-values), governed by
4120   the exact gauge; the carrier/fiber rescaling reduces the residue reading to cell arithmetic.


4121   44    Hodge Connection
4122   The loss-ledger ↔ cycle-filtration correspondence signature-based cycle detection of §40 is preliminary;
4123   calibrating it (hodge_layer_calib.py) surfaced a structural question out of scope here. The
4124   carrier’s descent 3D → 2D → 1D books a loss ledger — height (ordinate), radius, angle — and its
4125   leading central jet factors, by BSD/Gross–Zagier [23, 24], into three invariants the census resolves
4126   independently: the order 𝑟 (vanishing multiplicity), the regulator Reg (the height/Abel–Jacobi datum),
4127   and |Sha| (the local–global obstruction). So each of three cycle-filtration layers ordinarily invisible
4128   to Hodge projection carries a distinct retained coordinate — a genuinely different phenomenon from
4129   the Hodge-visible detection, and the reason those results are marked preliminary. The organising
4130   principle is that no layer should remain invisible. This is theorem-level for semisimple carrier states,
4131   where the moment tower is jointly faithful (§44.1), and is the target for extension classes. Beyond |Sha|,
4132   the transcendental Ceresa/Gross–Schoen class — the modified diagonal in CH2 (𝐶 3 )0 , homologically
4133   trivial — is the tensor-cube test case for the derivative/height tower, where its Beilinson–Bloch

                                                           111
4134   height is related, in the relevant theorem-anchored triple-product settings, to a central 𝐿-derivative
4135   of 𝐻 1 (𝐶)⊗3 (Zhang [26]; Yuan–Zhang–Zhang [27]); the classical hyperelliptic control vanishes,
4136   while known nontrivial Ceresa/Gross–Schoen examples provide positive level-three controls. Its
4137   exact carrier landing and extension-tower faithfulness are developed in the companion paper [30]
4138   — not proved here. Initial results appear to affirm this (hodge_griffiths_probe.py, App. B): the
4139   regulator/value channel fires for every homologically-trivial cycle in the census (no silent cycle),
4140   and the recursive tower already shows cycles absent at level one appearing at level ≥ 2. The
4141   companion paper [30] carries out the full correspondence: a from-scratch triple-product central
4142   derivative landing the Ceresa height, the exact coupling that induces each higher Griffiths layer,
4143   and the ledger ↔ Bloch–Beilinson-graded bĳection. (Status at this draft: the depth dictionary and
4144   semisimple theorem are machine-checked there; the Ceresa computation’s 𝐿-side is on record — the
4145   Klein quartic’s Ceresa channel carries forced sign −1 and central derivative 0.8299 ≠ 0, matching
4146   the known non-torsion of the cycle — with the height side open; and the first unnamed rung,
4147   grade four, is mapped and crossed on the carrier.) A further probe against a deeper cycle-filtration
4148   example produced the expected delayed tower signature 0, . . . , 0, ≠ 0: a class silent at depth 1 first
4149   fires at depth 2, recomputed from point-counting, its first nonzero slot matching the expected tower
4150   level of the class (tower_exhaustion_test.py, App. B). Define the carrier filtration by vanishing of
4151   the tower readouts 𝑇𝑗 ,
                                         𝑑
                                       𝐹car := { 𝑧 : 𝑇0 (𝑧) = · · · = 𝑇𝑑−1 (𝑧) = 0 },
4152   with no reference to any Bloch–Beilinson depth (non-circular by construction). On this definition the
4153   depth correspondence is a theorem, machine-checked in Lean (RequestProject/HodgeLedgerFiltration.lean:

4158   (firstVisibleDepth_eq_grade), the depth unique (isFirstVisible_unique) and preserved by

4160   since 𝐹car is defined by vanishing of the tower readouts, the depth correspondence is definitional
4161   bookkeeping, exact by construction — their value is that transport-invariance and the conditional
4162   identification below attach to a non-circular, machine-fixed object, not that the correspondence
4163   is itself deep. Moreover 𝐹car is the unique filtration whose graded pieces are cut out by the tower
4164   (carrierFiltration_unique); consequently, whenever a Bloch–Beilinson filtration exists with those
4165   universal properties on the source class, it coincides with 𝐹car (blochBeilinson_coincides) —
4166   a conditional corollary that assumes no general existence of the (conjectural) Bloch–Beilinson
4167   filtration, which is stronger and cleaner than positing that existence. Two inputs are not carried here
4168   for the full extension/cycle class — the semisimple half being unconditional (below) — and are the
4169   spine of the companion paper: joint faithfulness of the derivative/height tower, equivalently the no-
4170   silent-layer statement 𝑧 ≠ 0 ⇒ ∃𝑑, 𝑇𝑑 (𝑧) ≠ 0 on extension data (Exhaustive; supported numerically
4171   by hodge_griffiths_probe.py and tower_exhaustion_test.py, not proved on extension data),
4172   and the from-scratch triple-product central-derivative identity landing the Ceresa/Gross–Schoen
4173   height at level three (whose derivative-to-height step consumes Zhang [26] / Yuan–Zhang–
4174   Zhang [27]). Each arithmetic landing invoked is theorem-anchored — Tate and Gross–Zagier–
4175   Kolyvagin [24, 25] at depth one, the Gross–Schoen/Ceresa triple-product bridge at tensor depth
4176   three ([26, 27]). So the depth correspondence is a machine-checked theorem for the carrier
4177   filtration 𝐹car and a conditional corollary for Bloch–Beilinson. The no-silent-layer input is precisely

                                                         112
       triviality of the carrier radical 𝑅 := 𝑑 ker 𝑇𝑑 (exhaustive_of_radical_trivial), which reduces
                                             Ñ
4178

4179   gradewise to a nondegeneracy obligation — a faithful regulator into an anisotropic height pairing
4180   (grade_visible_of_nondegenerate), discharged by Néron–Tate positivity at depth one.

4181   44.1   Cycle-filtration faithfulness: the semisimple theorem and the Ceresa frontier
4182   The structural half is unconditional.On the semisimple carrier state — the finite duality-stable weight
4183   fiber, an amplitude state 𝑐 over distinct clock frequencies {𝜆 𝑖 } — the symmetric-power/moment
       tower 𝑇𝑑 (𝑐) = 𝑖 𝑐 𝑖 𝜆 𝑖𝑑 is a jointly faithful coordinate system: distinct frequencies make the
                         Í
4184

       moment matrix Vandermonde, so 𝑑 ker 𝑇𝑑 = 0 and every nonzero state fires at some fi-
                                                Ñ
4185

4186   nite level (CarrierTowerSeparation.momentTower_exhaustive, from momentTower_detects →
4187   momentTower_radical_trivial → exhaustive_of_radical_trivial; Lean). This is the finite-
4188   structural route — faithful carrier state → complete moment record → tower decomposition —
4189   carried out where it closes, discharging no-silent-layer unconditionally on the semisimple source
4190   class with no Bloch–Beilinson input. The scope is exactly that: the Vandermonde separation
4191   is a theorem about the weight-fiber amplitude state. A homologically-trivial cycle contributes,
4192   in the relevant Abel–Jacobi/motivic realization, extension data rather than merely a semisimple
4193   weight-fiber amplitude state — outside the reach of this theorem; whether the derivative/height
4194   tower is a jointly faithful coordinate system on that extension data — and hence whether 𝑅 = 0
4195   extends from the semisimple state to cycles — is the remaining problem, not settled here.
4196       We do not place the transcendental (Abel–Jacobi-trivial) Griffiths class in 𝑅: that would require
4197   every 𝑇𝑑 to factor through the conventional Abel–Jacobi realization (radical_of_factorsThrough).
4198   Since the global Gross–Schoen height carries non-archimedean arithmetic data
4199   (Zhang’s admissible/metrized-graph local terms [26]) absent from that single-archimedean realiza-
4200   tion, factorization through 𝐴𝐽C cannot be assumed, and ruling it out is itself a separate non-factorization
4201   theorem, not established here. Absent one, homological- and Abel–Jacobi-triviality is an adversarial
4202   no-silent-layer benchmark (not_mem_radical_of_detectedPast), not a proven ceiling. One rung of
4203   this is unconditional: for the Fermat quartic the Ceresa class [𝐶] − [𝐶 − ] is homologically trivial yet is
4204   detected by a nonzero harmonic volume, Harris’s Abel–Jacobi-type invariant (Harris [29]; Ceresa [28]
4205   for the generic curve), so ker(cl) ⊈ ker(𝐴𝐽C ) — a class closed in the homology readout fires at the next
4206   retained coordinate, no conjecture. This establishes exactly the first rung (past cl); it does not show
4207   the 𝐴𝐽C -kernel itself is penetrated by 𝑇3 . For that deeper rung the explicit evidence currently cuts
4208   the other way: in the explicit bielliptic Picard family with a closed-form height, the Beilinson–Bloch
4209   height of the Ceresa cycle is proportional to the Néron–Tate height of its Abel–Jacobi point, vanishing
4210   exactly when that point is torsion (Laga–Shnidman [31]) — the Beilinson–Bloch height is controlled
4211   by the associated Néron–Tate coordinate there, so it does not penetrate ker 𝐴𝐽C . The genuine
4212   deeper target is therefore a class with 𝐴𝐽C (𝑧) zero or torsion yet a nonzero arithmetic level-three
4213   invariant — necessarily one where the non-archimedean local height dominates (Zhang’s metrized-
4214   graph terms) or where the finer ℓ -adic/Galois Ceresa class, not the archimedean height, is the
4215   retained coordinate; that, with the from-scratch Ceresa landing, is the companion paper’s target [30].
4216




                                                          113
4217       Appendix
4218   Conclusion
4219   What stands, and at what strength. The carrier system of Part I is proven and machine-checked
4220   end to end: projection with its ledger is a bĳection, sources are synthesized from finite data alone,
4221   vanishing is exact focal cancellation, and the transport is universal and functorial. The 𝑆(𝑡) term is
4222   proven to be the registration gap between the scaled carrier and the unit chart — the chart-defect
4223   compensation mechanism, described and discharged. Symmetric-power functoriality holds at
4224   every rank with niceness discharged on the carrier, and Sato–Tate for Maass forms follows on
4225   the Galois-free route. Beyond Endoscopy’s uniformity problem is reduced to a single magnitude
4226   bound and its obstruction identified as the orbital transform’s own clock, with a repair that scales.
4227   The worked-example part retains two conditional GRH deductions and now states their minimal
4228   dependencies explicitly. The helix midpoint is a geometric output of unique area-law scale balance
4229   and no drift. A native 3D zero is a completed fibre focal cancellation at physical height 𝑍 > 0,
4230   exactly the analytic 𝐿-zero at 𝜎∗ + 𝑖 log 𝑍; its finite-bank detector is exactly equivalent to finite
4231   harmonic-pencil rank drop. Both Gram operators have 𝐺 ⊗ 𝐼3 spatial lifts that preserve and reflect
4232   rank drop. The scalar fibre 𝛾 idC is a valid local coordinate detector. Lean now also defines one
4233   fixed symmetric operator on the completed 3D event type, proves its explicit event eigenvectors,
4234   and packages the two resolvent versions: 3D-zero/eigenvector and 1D-zero/3D-zero/eigenvector.
4235   This event-space assembly does not by itself route an arbitrary analytic zero into the event subtype.
4236   Lean proves that the old 3D identity premise is GRH conjoined with midpoint-free native coverage;
4237   it also proves that the old 1D routing disjunction is automatic and that its pointwise chart-to-kernel
4238   premise alone implies the critical-line conclusion.
4239        The global 𝑆(𝑡) coordinate law remains an exact theorem: it carries the carrier-scale census to
4240   the unit-chart census and matches jumps, residues, and multiplicities. Completing the analytic-
4241   coverage route requires proving the resolvent/spectral capture for the fixed completed-event
                   (3)
4242   operator 𝐴 𝜒 , or instantiating the same interface with another fixed self-adjoint operator, as stated by
4243   grh_of_selfAdjoint_resolvent_capture. This separation preserves the proved carrier geometry
4244   and registration results while making the zero-set identification boundary explicit.
4245        The thesis, restated at the end as at the start: the unit-1 chart is the compression, not the object.
4246   Working in the scaled three-dimensional frame turned the 𝑆(𝑡) registration into a theorem, the
4247   convergence gate into a chart artifact, and a stalled trace-formula estimate into an exact gauge. The
4248   open research is the Hodge companion paper: the loss-ledger ↔ cycle-filtration correspondence,
4249   joint faithfulness on extension data, and the from-scratch Ceresa/Gross–Schoen landing (§44.1).
4250   Everything else that remains is bookkeeping at its own site: the Lean formalization scope is recorded
4251   where the theorems live (§37, Prop. 55). The theorems are checked and the artifacts are public.


4252   A    The exact gauge on the archimedean uniformity
4253   Altuğ [2, 3, 4] executes Beyond Endoscopy for GL(2) and the standard representation. Its analytic
4254   core is a uniformity estimate: after the arithmetic weights 𝐿(1, 𝜒𝐷 ) are expanded by an approximate
4255   functional equation and the trace variable is Poisson-summed, one must bound, uniformly in
4256   (𝜉, 𝜈, 𝑙, 𝑓 , 𝑋), the Fourier transform 𝐽𝑙, 𝑓 (𝜉, 𝜈, 𝑋) of a product of a fixed cutoff 𝐺 and a smoothed
4257   orbital transform (Prop. 5.2, Part III); Altuğ calls the 𝐶, 𝐷-independence of the implied constant
4258   “the central issue” [3, App. A]. The transform whose asymptotics drive the appendix is (Part II,

4296   This identification is a direct comparison of Taylor data, needing no appeal to uniqueness of the
4297   asymptotic expansion — whose coefficients 𝐴±𝑚 (𝐶 2 𝐷) are in any case not constant in 𝐷, depending

4300   endpoint Taylor datum of the same amplitude, the (2 − 𝑡)𝑢/2 factor supplying the 𝑢/2-dependence.

4302   term by term, so 𝑏 𝑚 (𝑢) = 𝑐 𝑚± (𝑢/2) directly.

4331   (𝑙 𝑓 2 / 𝑋)𝑁−𝑀+3 . We carry this power-counting only to the point where each inner bound reduces,
4332   term by term, to the single magnitude estimate of Lemma 81 — the exact-gauge substitute for
4333   Altuğ’s oscillation estimate, which is the sole change from his Proposition 5.2 — whose constants
4334   𝐵𝜏,𝑚,𝑎 (Φ) and ∥𝐺 (𝑖) ∥ ∞ are finite and independent of (𝜉, 𝜈, 𝑙, 𝑓 , 𝑋); the full exponent bookkeeping is
4335   his.                                                                                                    □
4336       Every uniform constant in §A is one application of Lemma 81; the content of Altuğ’s Appendix A,
4337   from the exact-gauge standpoint, is that single magnitude estimate. Where Altuğ’s route controls the
4338   transform through the asymptotic expansion together with an oscillation bound on the remainder,
4339   the exact gauge replaces that oscillation bound by the triangle inequality in the coordinate that
4340   makes the integrand real: the whole (𝜉, 𝜈, 𝑙, 𝑓 , 𝑋)-uniformity then rests on the 𝑥-independence of
4341   the single line integral 𝐵𝜏,𝑚,𝑎 (Φ), with no cancellation estimate at any step.


4342   B    Reproducibility
4343   Every measured statement is produced by a self-contained script (no 𝐿-function library); the values
4344   quoted in the text are reproduced below with the script that computes each.
4345   • Lemma 81 (the gauge bound), be_uniformity_certify.py. For a Gaussian Φ, 𝐵1,0,1 (Φ) = 0.686,
4346     and the certificate margin 𝑀(𝑥) = |𝐴(𝑥)| 𝑥 𝜏/2 /𝐵 satisfies sup𝑥 𝑀(𝑥) = 0.914 ≤ 1, uniformly across
4347     𝑥 = 𝐶 2 𝐷 ∈ [0.05, 2500] and (𝜏, 𝑚) ∈ {0.5, 1, 2, 4} × {0, 2}. The line integrand decays as 𝑒 −𝜋|𝑣|
4348     (𝑣 → +∞) and 𝑒 −𝜋|𝑣|/2 (𝑣 → −∞), so 𝐵𝜏,𝑚,𝑎 (Φ) < ∞ for every 𝜏 > 0.
4349   • Proposition 84 (the uniform constant), be_prop52_certify.py. The constant 𝐿 𝑀 = ∥𝜕𝑦𝑀 (𝐺(𝑦/𝑋) 𝑦 Ψ)∥ 𝐿1
4350     fits a uniform monomial 𝐿 𝑀 ∼ 𝐶 𝑀 (𝑙 𝑓 2 )𝑎 𝑀 (1 + 𝜉)𝑏 𝑀 𝑋 𝑔 𝑀 with 𝑎 𝑀 = 0.41, 0.05, −0.05 for 𝑀 = 1, 2, 3
4351     and 𝑏 𝑀 ≤ 0. The 𝑙 𝑓 2 -exponent 𝑎 𝑀 grows more slowly than 𝑀 (𝑑𝑎/𝑑𝑀 ≈ −0.23), so each
4352     integration by parts nets 𝜈−1 and the bound is summable — the standard-representation side
4353     of the productivity boundary. (This is the crude magnitude route; the sharp exponents of
4354     Proposition 84 follow from Theorem 82.)
4355   • The registration instruments (§9.8), st_mu6_gram.py, st_cf_lags.py, st_cell_phase.py. Four
4356     pre-registered tests of positional coupling between the zero events and the lattice layers, all
4357     null, as the proven ergodicity predicts. (1) Gram parity: violation rates 0.0728 vs 0.0720 at
4358     𝑁=5000 ticks — flat. (2) mod-6 alignment of the Gram defect: the run-1 signal (𝑝 = 0.0355,
4359     IID permutation, 𝑁=1200) fails to replicate under the autocorrelation-preserving circular-shift
4360     null at 𝑁=5000 (𝑝 = 0.058 full range, 𝑝 = 0.49 upper half); the IID null overstates significance
4361     for Rosser-block-correlated sequences — the circular shift is the correct null for alignment
4362     tests. (3) CF lags {7, 106, 113} (the 𝜋-convergent denominators): 66th percentile, 𝑝 = 0.32; the
4363     visible autocorrelation is short-range spacing rigidity. (4) Cell-phase kinks: the zeros’ phases
4364     𝑥 = frac(𝜃(𝛾)/𝜋) follow the smooth classical 𝑆-shape (mean 0.4980, the half-jump shift); density
4365     kinks at the carrier subdivision 𝑥 = 1/3, 2/3 are smaller than at control breakpoints (0.0396 vs
4366     0.0477). Method laws recorded: sampling at the chart’s own ticks aliases the carrier subdivision
4367     away (instruments must sample the carrier coordinate); and positional statistics test a claim the
4368     ontology disclaims — the 𝜋/3 claim is cancellation at events, never placement of events.

4369   • The emergent clock (§30), mb_beat.py. The script scans the clock coordinate 𝜈clock = 2𝜈𝐽 , so
4370     its profile is 𝑒(−𝑦𝜈clock /4𝑙 𝑓 2 ) while the analytic 𝐽 of Prop. 84 uses 𝑒(−𝑦𝜈𝐽 /2𝑙 𝑓 2 ). The current
4371     estimator fits the continuous log-power profile log |𝑉(𝜈clock )| 2 with a degree-7 envelope plus
4372     the first two harmonics sharing one fundamental; the error audit compares one, two, and three
4373     harmonics. In that coordinate the fitted clock law is Δ𝜈clock = 0.524(𝑙 𝑓 2 )1.03 (𝑋/8)−1.04 (1 + 𝜉)0.00
4374     with 𝑅 2 = 1.000; equivalently Δ𝜈𝐽 = 12 Δ𝜈clock . Per-cell 𝜅 eff = 4𝑙 𝑓 2 /(𝑋Δ𝜈clock ) has mean 0.943,
4375     standard deviation 0.025, and range 0.895–0.971; the harmonic-truncation median period shift is
4376     2.4 × 10−4 (largest 6.7 × 10−3 on the weakest long-period cell). The legacy deep-dip estimator
4377     gave 0.533(𝑙 𝑓 2 )1.00 (𝑋/8)−0.98 (1 + 𝜉)0.02 at 𝑅 2 = 0.996. The rank sweep mb_beat.py ranks 13
4378     applies the same 𝑈𝑟 (𝑥) multiplier for 0 ≤ 𝑟 ≤ 13 and separates two masks: continuous clock
4379     cells and deep-event cells. On clock cells every rank has 𝑅 2 = 1.000, 𝑙 𝑓 2 -exponent 1.03–1.04, and
4380     𝑋-exponent −1.04–−1.03. The continuous clock is present in all 12 nonzero-𝜉 cells through 𝑟 = 9,
4381     then in 10, 9, 8, 8 cells for 𝑟 = 10, 11, 12, 13; deep productivity drops faster, from 10/12 at 𝑟 = 0 to
4382     3/9 and 3/8 at 𝑟 = 11, 12. Thus the high-rank degradation is event visibility, not a breakdown of
4383     the clock law. The Beyond-Endoscopy scaling test is therefore cell-wise: first certify the phase
4384     clock on each cell, then measure the productive deep-event yield inside the certified cells. The
4385     same run confirms that the deep-dip comb vanishes at 𝜉 = 0 for 𝑟 = 0 (the integrand is unimodal
4386     there).
4387   • The GL(3) clock lift, mb_gl3_clock_lift.py, mb_gl3_wall_lift.py, gl3_family.py. The
4388     GL(3) lift keeps the clock law but does not keep it as one scalar MB clock: the two trace
4389     coordinates carry separate clocks, and the diagonal readout combines them as 𝑄/(𝑆 𝑎 + 𝑆𝑏 ). The
4390     split-coordinate clock ratios are pinned at median 1.0000, 1.0000, 1.0000 for the 𝑎-, 𝑏-, and diagonal
4391     readouts, while the same-𝑏 scalar collapse gives 0.8983. The wall-lift scan shows a persistent
4392     clock but only partial scalar compression of the spread (base 𝑅2 = 0.541, full scalar-feature
4393     𝑅2 = 0.623–0.640 on this grid). The family scan pins all four tested GL(3) forms, with universal
4394     cells 1.0005𝜋 and across-form spread 0.0001𝜋. Thus the higher-rank scaling rule is vector-clock
4395     extraction plus productivity accounting, not a single GL(2)-style period.
4396   • The formally proven GL(4) vector-clock scale audit, mb_scale_audit.py and TwoClockWeightLaw.lean.
4397     The audit composes the GL(2) rank sweep, the GL(3) split clock, and the GL(4) three-coordinate
4398     vector-clock theorem. In Lean, gl4_trace_window_vector_clock proves that three independent
4399     trace spans force Δ𝑖 = 𝑄/𝑆 𝑖 on the three trace coordinates and force the locked diagonal readout
4400     Δdiag = 𝑄/(𝑆 𝑎 + 𝑆𝑏 + 𝑆 𝑐 ); gl4_scalar_collapse_not_uniform proves that scalar collapse across
4401     distinct spans is obstructed exactly by span inequality. For GL(2), the clock law is certified
4402     at 𝑅 2 ≥ 0.999 for 14/14 ranks while productive deep-cell yield ranges from 0.33 to 0.83. For
4403     GL(3), the vector clock passes 24/24 𝑎-cells, 24/24 𝑏-cells, and 24/24 diagonal cells, while the
4404     anisotropic same-clock control has median 0.7966 on the 𝑏-axis. For GL(4), the vector clock
4405     passes 36/36 cells on each of the 𝑎, 𝑏, 𝑐 trace coordinates and 36/36 diagonal cells; the scalar
4406     controls have medians 0.9715 and 0.9319 on anisotropic 𝑏- and 𝑐-windows, confirming the formal
4407     scalar-collapse obstruction and preserving the vector readout as the scaling law. The productivity
4408     ledger records the measured wall accounting alongside the formal clock theorem: visible wall
4409     cells are 109/144, coherent-envelope cells 76/144, and near-vector productive cells 28/144.
